Current Commentary

The German-Austrian Customs Union Issue 6

The German-Austrian Customs Union issue is currently awaiting mediation by the League of Nations Council. Therefore, whether the relationship between Germany, Austria, and France will be restored or broken will depend on the situation at the future meeting. However, judging from the words and actions of both sides, there is a trend of increasing danger. For example, after the French Prime Minister's speech in Conflans stating that France would hardly tolerate the German-Austrian Customs Union, German public opinion strongly criticized it. The more radical ones advocated urging the government to change its foreign policy and withdraw from the League of Nations. Even the more moderate ones expressed dissatisfaction with France. This shows that their feelings are not harmonious, as evidenced by their speeches. As for the measures taken by both sides, they are economically linked. Germany and Austria want to unite Italy, Russia, Turkey, and other countries to form a faction, while France is allied with the Little Entente countries to form a faction. This is already obvious. According to reports from Rome, the foreign ministers of the Little Entente are secretly meeting in Rome, and the King of Romania and the head of Yugoslavia suddenly met on the Danube River, reportedly to discuss the German-Austrian Customs Union. According to reports from Geneva, the Soviet Union and Turkey have expressed their unwillingness to participate in the European Federation conference to discuss European economic matters. Much can be studied from these subtle clues, which are not unrelated to the actions taken by both sides to deal with the customs union. We have received important domestic telegrams.

Entrance of Various Representatives into the Grand Auditorium 7

To fully understand the value of unity and peace and its impact on the future survival of the nation, we should further analyze the international and domestic actual environments, understand the strengths and weaknesses of others, and examine ourselves. This is essential for national planning. Please first observe the international trends, with particular emphasis on their economic development aspects.

(I) The widespread international crisis at present is the economic panic, with the number of unemployed increasing endlessly. Overproduction is a hidden worry for most people. The increase in production in European, American, and Japanese countries after the Great War is an obvious fact. However, if we say that production has reached the point of oversupply, then why have workers and farmers in various countries not been able to enjoy a living standard above a certain level? There are certainly many specialized reasons for disputes, but the main problem lies in the uneven distribution. If this system does not change, then the goods of European, American, and Japanese countries would rather see a portion of their own people lack enjoyment, but for economic benefits, they must transfer it to other countries. Since this distribution system is difficult to change in the short term, the economic aggression of imperialism is also difficult to stop. This is why China, with its backward industry and weak economic resistance, is a cause for concern.

(II) The above is regarding capitalist countries. Even regarding Soviet Russia, which advocates communism, when its Five-Year Plan is completed, it will also be a new force in the world market. With a total mobilization of over 130 million people and the use of 80 trillion rubles of capital, the entire Russian agricultural and industrial fields will be transformed into collective, scientific production, and its scale will be considerable. If it succeeds, its productivity will not be easily underestimated. Now, Soviet Russia is further shortening the five-year period to four years to complete it as soon as possible. Just considering the cotton production business it operates in Central Asia, its rapid progress in quantity will inevitably make China the end point. Moreover, the new road of 1,445 kilometers surrounding the Xinjiang border to connect with the Siberian trunk line was completed last year. Together with the Middle East Railway, which penetrates our Northeast, they form a constant mountain snake force, with a vast territory stretching for thousands of miles. The Chinese people should pay serious attention to all aspects of military, economic, and propaganda.

As for the general trend of politics and military affairs in European, American, and Japanese countries, there is no need to list them one by one. At least in the past five years, the political and military issues between European and American countries are still under the control of economic issues. Whether the reduction of armaments can be successful, especially whether the naval allocation problem can be satisfactorily resolved, as well as France's border defense and Italy's overseas development, all relate to the general trend of international peace. The situation of armed peace in the world has become an undeniable fact. Our country, based on its deep love of peace, sincerely hopes for world peace. But in the unlikely event that a war breaks out internationally, our country should at the very least have sufficient self-defense preparations and further seek to advance its international position. In today's world, our compatriots should constantly pay attention to the international environment to seek a deep understanding and plan for the country's adaptation.

Looking back at the domestic actual environment, we cannot help but feel ashamed and saddened. However, the sick should not avoid doctors. Scientific research should first take facts as the object. China is poor and weak, with hundreds of holes and thousands of sores, and unemployment and backward production are the biggest problems. The lack of popular education, the lack of political experience, and the lack of self-government habits are also important obstacles on the path of national progress. The current evolution of Chinese society is still in the early stages of the European Industrial Revolution, while others have progressed for more than a century. The largest part of what replaces China's handicraft industry is not the domestic machine industry, but the machine industry of other countries. The largest part of those who compete with Chinese labor are not Chinese capital, but the capital of other countries. The country itself

Page 8

Statistical undertakings have developed relatively late, and frequent military affairs have led to the fact that sharp industry surveys have not yet been carried out. The total number should be able to drive any country in the world by several times. Just based on what is seen in various places, bandits and vagrants are all unemployed people who have been excluded from the industrial revolution. Foreign factories have taken away their handicraft livelihoods, and the country has no factories to accommodate them. In addition, floods, droughts, famines, and wars have made the unemployed more numerous, and social stability has also been shaken as a result. Every time I think about the situation of backward production in China, if the facts were not all there, I would almost not be able to believe it. China has a population of over 400 million and a land area of over 10,735,454 square kilometers, but the total length of railways in the country is only 12,335 kilometers. Highways have only developed in recent years, and are only 51,210 kilometers, most of which are still dirt roads. Shipping routes, including coastal and inland rivers, are only 12,988 kilometers. The total number of merchant ships is only 439,617 tons, of which British and Japanese foreign merchants operate 326,137 tons. There are also foreign merchants from Norway and other countries with irregular ships of 236,000 tons that have not been included. There is nothing more to say about foreign shipping. As for the national shipbuilding capacity, it is only 10,000 tons per year. There are only 91,130 kilometers of wired telephone lines. There are only 1,105 telegraph offices, averaging one telegraph office for every two counties. There are only a little over 110 wireless machines besides military use. Although there are recently two air routes between Shanghai-Yichang and Beijing, there are only 20 airplanes. The total number of mine workers in the country, including salt mine workers, is estimated to be about one million. As for other factories that can truly use machines to produce on a considerable scale, the number of workers employed is not even close to this. In terms of domestic factory capital, foreign capital is several times that of Chinese capital. Since the tariff autonomy this year, foreign merchants have also changed their investment methods to add factories in China. Since February, the number of factories added by foreign merchants has been as high as about 600, which is also a new trend of economic aggression. If Chinese merchants in industries such as tobacco and cloth are failing day by day, then foreign capital is becoming more prosperous. China claims to be a large and resource-rich country, but the ability of the Chinese people to develop and their entrepreneurial skills are both undeniably weak. Goods are discarded on the ground and supplies are relied upon from others. For example, the imported coal in the 19th year was 2,467,042 tons, with a value of 24,919,475 customs taels, and steel was 8,846,760 dan, with a value of 56,564,903 taels. The total number of kerosene was 185,608,596 gallons, with a total value of 54,864,546 taels. These are all necessary natural products. There is no need to mention that cotton textiles, woolen textiles, etc., are major imports. As a country that claims to be based on agriculture, the value of imported grains in the 18th year was over 14.3 million customs taels, and the value of imported foreign sugar was over 91 million taels. In the 19th year, the value of imported grains was over 13.4 million customs taels, and the value of imported foreign sugar was over 86 million taels. The average annual import tax is over 200 million taels. With backward industries to this extent, only the joint efforts of the government and the people to actively create products can be enough to survive. In terms of education, according to the statistics of the 17th year, the number of students in universities and specialized schools nationwide was 19,453, and the number of middle school students was 234,811. Even in terms of middle school students, there must be an average of one person out of every 1,700 people. The number of elementary school students was over 7 million, but the number of school-age children who did not attend school was still over 35 million. It is estimated that the national illiteracy rate is 80 percent. If the situation of traffic congestion, backward production, and lack of popular education is not fundamentally addressed through a considerable period of time, even with the wisdom of sages, it will be difficult to plan for the country. Zhongzheng lists these facts not to make compatriots feel discouraged, but only the brave can recognize the truth of the facts, and only the wise can seek a way out from the facts. The current objective environment is as difficult as it was in the past few years. The only difference is the situation of unity and peace. Unity and peace cannot be separated. If the overall situation of the country can be taken into consideration and there is a considerable period of time for it to proceed step by step calmly, not only can the government show the effectiveness of construction, but also the capital invested in private businesses will rise like the wind and clouds and cooperate to advance. It goes without saying that foreign capital will be utilized. The people have long hoped for the stability of order. Now, our National Revolutionary Army has offered unity and peace to the people with great sacrifices and long-term struggles. How should the people cherish and protect unity and peace to seek a way out for China, seek China's construction in unity and peace, and seek the survival of the nation and individuals in unity and peace? With firm aspirations and full effort, all those who support unity and peace are considered public friends of the nation, and those who undermine unity and peace are considered public enemies. If we persevere with sincerity and perseverance, the current factual environment will inevitably be conquered, and the prosperity of the country and the happiness of the people will be just around the corner.

Now, the gentlemen of the National Assembly are elected by the people to plan for the survival of the country and the nation in the capital. The gentlemen are all elites from all walks of life, but what the gentlemen should consider is the problem of the entire nation, not the problem of a certain sector. The gentlemen come from all parts of the country and overseas, but what the gentlemen are discussing is the problem of the entire country, not the problem of a certain region. The method of planning for the country should focus on the main points, and the focus should be on the big picture. With the virtue and ability of the gentlemen, they should be able to have foresight, without the need for Zhongzheng's humble suggestions. However, the stability of national order, the establishment of national consensus, the development of national economy and people's livelihood, and the implementation of construction plans all depend on the gentlemen's deliberations and rely on the gentlemen to set an example for all compatriots, to change the atmosphere and correct people's hearts. I dare to hope that the gentlemen will pay special attention to the major issues of the constitution and the procedures for industrial construction. The constitution is to establish a consensus and stabilize people's hearts to establish a norm for political and social progress. Only by putting the country on track can the chaos outside the track be eliminated. Zhongzheng believes that this matter is the important mission of the National Assembly, and has repeatedly insisted on it, causing misunderstanding among friends who are usually respected and loved. In fact, there is more than enough pain in my heart. Since the meaning of the constitution is important beyond the norm, its articles should also be simple, practical, and easy to implement. Do not rely on high-sounding words, but seek appropriateness. Do not seek to be different, but seek feasibility. After it is established, the government and the people must establish a heart that is as unshakable as a mountain and have the attitude of sunshine.

Cars Outside the Meeting Hall Door 8

Unify the degree and abide by it consistently so that China can achieve governance and peace. As for the procedures for industrial construction, they are also necessary at present. In terms of China's current industrial situation, there is nothing that does not need construction. In terms of China's talent and economy, taking care of everything will inevitably lead to nothing being accomplished. Determine the order of priority and establish a procedure, without extravagance, but limit it to what can be done on a regular basis, and do our best to devote the government and the people to it. As for how to determine and encourage production while at the same time taking into account labor welfare and not going against the economic policy of the People's Livelihood Principle, how to promote education so that it can take into account the livelihood of the people, these kinds of questions are all what the country requires the gentlemen to think deeply about to establish a new foundation for national rejuvenation in history.

To seek the governance of the country, there must be a definite belief, a summary plan, and a unified pace. The Prime Minister advocated the theory of knowing is difficult and doing is easy, which is the only needle to save China's traditional decadent mentality and the only plan to restore the nation's enterprising vitality. Today, the meeting place that we can entrust to gather for discussion is only based on an engineer's design, and it can only be completed on schedule by countless bricklayers and lumberjacks working day and night according to the pre-determined drawings. There is absolutely no reason in the world that engineers gather and fight while workers stand by and watch, so that any building can be completed. The way to build a country is the same. The only principle of building China is the Prime Minister's doctrine, the Prime Minister's strategy, and all the Prime Minister's teachings. If we try to carefully examine and think deeply about it, what doctrine is great, profound, and suitable for China like the Three People's Principles? What strategy is broad, detailed, lofty, and practical like the Prime Minister's hand-determined Outline of National Reconstruction and the Great Outline of National Reconstruction? If it were not from a national leader who is immortal for thousands of years, upholding the spirit of the world for the public and the unchanging will through the ages, then what proposition would be sufficient to give life to the nation's faith, arouse the world's respect, and make hundreds of millions of martyrs break their necks and break their bellies to go to it without regret? Therefore, accepting the Prime Minister's teachings and faithfully striving to carry them out is the way for our Chinese nation to save itself. Now, the country is re-looking at the prosperity of unity and the light of peace. There are many heavy burdens from inheriting the great and throwing in the difficult. However, if we can proceed step by step, we can also move day by day to the realm of construction, perfection, and constitutional completion. Which Chinese does not want long-term stability and advancement to survive? However, long-term stability must be based on long-term peace, and survival depends on advancement. Political phenomena often express the meaning of physical and psychological stability, such as long-term chaos will not produce people, and forgetting chaos must know that liking chaos becomes a habit, and liking governance also becomes a habit. The Chinese people should transform the psychology of liking chaos into the perseverance of seeking governance. Knowing only to hope for governance but not seeking governance will lead to no day of governance. Although the governance, chaos, prosperity, and change of a country are often tied to the psychology of a few who can change the atmosphere, let alone the many talents selected by the national people. The future of the country and the nation is tied to the gentlemen of the National Assembly. Only the representatives can plan together.

Hu Shuhua's Speech 9

Representative Hu Shuhua said, Chairman of the National Government, Central Committee members, representatives, and guests, today is the National Government of the Republic of China, following the Prime Minister's teachings and planning for national unity and construction, convening the National Assembly. At the opening of this solemn and great National Assembly, recalling the Prime Minister's will at the time of his death (the recent advocacy for convening the National Assembly and abolishing unequal treaties must be implemented in the shortest possible time), every time we held a memorial week, we would recite it until it was realized now. In addition to being pleased, recalling the many difficulties and hardships in the past six years, relying on the efforts of the Central Committee, representatives from all over the country are able to meet here to express their opinions. This is what the representatives of various provinces and cities should thank the Central Committee for. Recently, the imperialist newspapers spread rumors about whether the National Assembly could be convened. Considering their intentions, after the opening of the National Assembly, they will abolish unequal treaties. Recently, the chairman reported that political aggression is extremely terrible. After the opening of the National Assembly, if the powers cannot automatically abolish them, we will definitely make proper methods so that they will have to abolish them. The general public has been raining for days, thinking that the National Assembly should be clear on the day of opening. In fact, the wind and rain in recent days are just expressing the wind and rain. We should work together in the same boat and expect that there will be a lot of sunshine when the official meeting is held, and the blue sky and white sun will shine all over the world. I wish the success of the National Assembly (applause from the crowd).

Important Domestic Telegrams 2

A Glimpse of the Meeting Place Situation 12

(Nanjing) In addition to the Central Committee members and National Committee members, there were more than 450 representatives attending the opening of the National Assembly. The first row downstairs was Jiang Zhongzheng, Zhang Xueliang, Dai Jitao, Yu Youren, He Yingqin, Ma Fuxiang, etc. Foreign guests sat opposite the first row, and the representatives of each province sat in the seats downstairs. The colorfulness of their costumes was truly remarkable, and the Tibetan Living Buddha Panchen Lama, wearing yellow satin all over his body, sat in the guest seat upstairs, dazzlingly interesting. Mrs. Jiang, Song Meiling, was also in the guest seat listening, with a natural attitude and a smiling face (Special Telegram on the 5th).

(Nanjing) More than 450 representatives have arrived today, only 60 short, because most of the representatives from Sichuan and the representatives from Qian and Gui are still on the way (Special Telegram on the 5th).

Worshipping at the Mausoleum and Taking the Oath This Morning 13

(Nanjing) The Preparatory Committee decided to sign the seat tomorrow morning at 10:00 a.m. and worship at the Mausoleum tomorrow morning at 8:00 a.m. It was initially proposed to take the oath today. Some people said that taking the oath tomorrow morning when worshipping at the Mausoleum would be more solemn (Special Telegram on the 5th).

Panchen Lama's Eulogy 14

(Nanjing) Panchen Erdeni sent an eulogy saying, today is the opening of the National Assembly. Panchen, as a remote person from the western border, is honored to be able to participate in the grand meeting and meet with the representatives of the whole country. Chairman Jiang of our country, following the Prime Minister's doctrine, completed the full achievements of the revolution. He is working hard on political training and construction. The era of constitutional government is about to be completed. He is inheriting the Prime Minister's teachings, convening the National Assembly, consulting the heroes of the group, and cooperating to discuss national affairs, formulating a constitution to permanently solidify the country. It is seen that the blue sky and white sun will always promote the glory of China. The Three People's Principles and Five Powers will always be the model for the world. Panchen is looking at the border situation and speaking his sincere thoughts, thinking of opening the government's long-term plan to quickly save the Tibetan people from misery. He has been running north and south, and his mind and energy are exhausted. Recently, the Kangzang people have been appealing for peace, and he has been deeply compassionate. He hopes that all the gentlemen will broadly relieve the great discussion, rectify the border, follow the Prime Minister's teaching of helping the weak and supporting the weak, consolidate the basis of the country's sovereignty and territory, reassert the prestige of the upper country, and do not abandon the treasures of the West. This is what Panchen is raising his hands and celebrating and sincerely praying for (Special Telegram on the 5th).

Banquet of the Lizi Society 15

Mr. and Mrs. Chiang Kai-shek as Hosts

Representative Lin Presents Chiang with a Cane

(Nanjing) Tonight at seven o'clock, a banquet was held in the auditorium of the Lizi Society. 550 representatives and guests attended, seated at six rows of tables. Mr. and Mrs. Chiang Kai-shek sat opposite each other in the main seats on the stage. Among the female guests were Zhang Mojun and sixteen others, and among the male guests were eighteen, including Dai Jitao, Zhang Xueliang, He Yingqin, Ma Fuxiang, Liu Luyin, and Yang Shuzhuang. Hu Shuhua was in the first seat. Chiang Kai-shek delivered a speech, and the reception was simple due to the haste of the arrangements. The representatives, having come to represent the people, respectfully offered a toast to his health. Then, Representative Lin from Honolulu presented Chiang Kai-shek with a cane, as a piece of ragtime music was played. Chiang Kai-shek, after receiving it, smiled and said, "Does the esteemed representative wish to use this cane to defeat imperialism and abolish unequal treaties?" The crowd applauded. Then, representatives from Shanghai and Liaoning delivered speeches. Finally, a film about the ancient events of the French Revolution in Marseille was shown, and the event concluded. (5th dispatch)

Not Many Proposals from Representatives 16

(Nanjing) The representatives from various provinces have prepared many proposals. Even the representatives from the Northeast have prepared twenty to thirty proposals. Representatives from other provinces and cities have also prepared many proposals. However, because eighty people are required to co-sign, and the proposals must also be reviewed by the review committee, only a few can be listed on the agenda. In addition, most of the conversations among the representatives focus on local or regional issues, which do not seem necessary to be raised at the People's Congress. Therefore, it is known that even fewer proposals can be submitted for general review. (5th dispatch)

Zhang Xueliang's Proposal 17

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang's proposal is based on the principles of the Provisional Constitution and focuses on two aspects: education and the people's livelihood, forming two proposals: (1) Popular Education, (2) Industrial Construction, totaling several thousand words. (5th dispatch)

Responsibilities of the Presidium 18

Revised Text of the National Assembly Organization Law

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 5th to revise and promulgate Article 4 of the National Assembly Organization Law. The revised text is as follows: Article 4. Those attending the National Assembly shall elect nine persons to form a presidium to manage the following matters. Unless otherwise stipulated in this law, decisions shall be made with the consent of more than half of the presidium members after deliberation: (1) Matters related to the special permissions in Clause 3 of the preceding article; (2) Matters related to the determination of the agenda, the conduct of discussions, and the arrangement of the agenda; (3) Matters related to the administration of the National Assembly; (4) Matters related to the protection and discipline of the representatives of the National Assembly.

Capital Celebration Assembly 19

Liu Luyin Delivers the Opening Speech

Wang Qi, Dai Fu-xian Deliver Speeches

(Nanjing) At 4 PM on the 5th, people from all walks of life in the capital held a celebration assembly for the National Assembly at the public sports ground. Over 20,000 people attended, including representatives of the National Assembly, party and government officials, military personnel, various organizations, and the general public. Liu Luyin, the chairman, delivered the opening speech, stating that since the Party overthrew the warlords, it has followed Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will to convene the National Assembly, hoping that the entire country would unite to take on the responsibility of national construction, establish a foundation for peaceful unification, and resolve to abolish all unequal treaties to enhance its international standing, so that the four issues of clothing, food, housing, and transportation for the 400 million compatriots can be satisfactorily resolved. Therefore, the entire people of Nanjing warmly welcome the representatives, and today's grand celebration expresses the infinite hope for the National Assembly. Next, Wang Qi, the Hunan representative to the National Assembly, delivered a speech, stating that the National Assembly aims to achieve unity and construction internally and abolish unequal treaties externally, which is of great significance, and the responsibilities of the representatives are extremely important. Currently, white imperialists are constantly aiming to harm our country, relying on unequal treaties as a shield to invade in every possible way, so the international status is very dangerous. The representatives should work together with the national people to seek the overall interests of the country, hoping that the meeting will achieve satisfactory results to live up to the expectations of the national people. Next, Dai Fu-xian, the representative of the Central National Government, delivered a speech, stating that the Party, under the leadership of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, struggled for many years before overthrowing the Qing Dynasty and establishing the Republic of China. Although the form of government changed at that time, the actual power still remained in the hands of warlords and bureaucrats. Therefore, Dr. Sun Yat-sen again led the compatriots across the country to work hard and struggled until he passed away due to overwork. When he was dying, he still eagerly hoped that his comrades would continue his will to complete the unification and construction of China to display the most glorious light of the past 5,000 years.

He also repeatedly instructed his comrades in his will to convene the National Assembly within the shortest possible time and strive to abolish unequal treaties. After Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death, the comrades of the Party followed his teachings and led the national people to work hard and struggled to eliminate the warlords who oppressed the people and the Communists who disrupted China. Although these achievements are the result of the sacrifices of armed comrades, the greatest strength still lies in the fact that the national compatriots can unanimously support the revolution, which is why we have today. Therefore, if we want to create a foundation for permanent peace and unity in the country in the future, we still need the people to be united in awareness and single-mindedness to achieve this goal. Now that the National Assembly has convened, its goals and tasks are extremely clear. After the Provisional Constitution is formulated and promulgated, the government should strive to achieve unification and construction based on this law, and the national people should also strive to realize it with the spirit of past struggles to create a new era and a new life for China. Finally, representatives from the city's Party headquarters, Lai Lian, and the city government, Xie Mindao, etc., delivered speeches and then shouted slogans, and the meeting concluded.

(5th dispatch)

Regulations of Various Committees 20

(Nanjing) Regulations of the Organizational Committees of the National Assembly (Chapter 1: General Provisions) Article 1. These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 13, Paragraph 2 of the National Assembly Organization Law. Article 2. The deliberations of each committee shall not involve matters beyond those entrusted by the National Assembly. Article 3. Each committee shall have a convener to organize the proceedings and maintain order. Article 4. The convener shall serve as the chairman of each committee's proceedings. Article 5. Each committee's proceedings shall not begin unless more than half of the members are present. Decisions shall be made with the consent of more than half of those present. If the votes are equal, the chairman shall decide. Article 6. If the cases reviewed by each committee are related to other committees, joint meetings may be held. The convener of the joint meeting shall serve as the chairman. Article 7. The results of each committee's review of cases shall be submitted in writing to the presidium within the time limit for submission to the plenary session for discussion. Article 8. Each committee meeting of this assembly may invite the proposer to attend and explain the purpose of the proposal. Article 9. The decisions of each review committee meeting shall not be announced to the public unless they have been submitted to the plenary session for decision and are considered to be confidential. Article 10. No member of each committee shall publicly express opinions on the cases submitted for review at any time. Article 11. Public attendance is prohibited at each committee meeting. Article 12. Unless otherwise stipulated in these regulations, the rules of procedure of the National Assembly shall be followed in each committee meeting. (Chapter 2: Representative Qualification Review Committee) Article 13. A representative qualification review committee shall be established in accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the National Assembly Organization Law. Its members and number shall be appointed by the presidium. Article 14. The review of representative qualifications shall be in accordance with the provisions of Articles 20 to 21 of the National Assembly Rules of Procedure. (Chapter 3: Proposal Review Committee) Article 15. A proposal review committee shall be established in accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the National Assembly Organization Law. Its members and number shall be appointed by the presidium. Article 16. The proposal review committee shall review the issues submitted to the National Assembly. Article 17. The proposal review committee shall review each issue in accordance with the provisions of Articles 41 and 42 of the National Assembly Rules of Procedure. Article 18. The proposal review committee may only decide whether or not it should become a proposal. It may not make substantive amendments without the consent of the presidium. (Chapter 4: Special Review Committee) Article 19. In accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the National Assembly Organization Law, the following special review committees may be established. Its members and number shall be appointed by the presidium: (1) Military Review Committee (2) Foreign Affairs Review Committee (3) Finance Review Committee (4) Legal System Review Committee (5) Economic Review Committee (6) Education Review Committee (7) Internal Affairs Review Committee Article 20. In addition to the committees listed in the preceding article, the presidium may, according to the characteristics of the cases under deliberation, designate members and organize a review committee to review them after the plenary session has decided. Article 21. The committees listed in Article 19 of these regulations shall review the following cases: (1) Those submitted by the plenary session for review (2) Those submitted directly by the presidium for review in accordance with the provisions of Article 4, Paragraph 1 of the National Assembly Rules of Procedure (Chapter 5: Affairs) Article 22. The minutes of each committee meeting, the drafting of documents, and other affairs shall be handled by the secretariat, which shall be equipped with a number of secretaries, a number of staff members, and a number of clerks. Article 23. The staff members in the preceding article shall handle affairs under the orders of the secretary-general and the conveners of each committee. (Chapter 6: Supplementary Provisions) Article 24. These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (6th dispatch)

Enthusiastic Celebrations in Various Places 22

Ping Celebration Meeting Passes Three Proposals

(Beiping) This morning at 9:00 AM, people from all walks of life in Beiping held a celebration meeting at Tiananmen to celebrate the opening of the National Assembly. More than 20,000 people participated. The entire city flew flags for one day. The city's Party headquarters chartered a streetcar to circulate propaganda materials around the city. A mat shed was erected high at the meeting place, with a portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and crossed Party and national flags. Zhou Xuechang, the chairman, reported that the opening of the National Assembly was to relieve our suffering. Our demands are to solve the people's livelihood, abolish consular jurisdiction, strive for construction, and promote international status. Zheng Guocai gave a speech expressing three hopes for the National Assembly: (1) Abide by the Provisional Constitution, (2) Promote unification, (3) Abolish unequal treaties. Wen Qun's representative, Hu Ruoyu, gave a speech saying that before today, the people had no meeting. Today, the people have a meeting, so it is worth celebrating. Then, three proposals were passed: (1) Send a telegram to the whole country to support the National Assembly, (2) Send a telegram to the National Assembly to automatically declare the abolition of consular jurisdiction and unequal treaties, (3) Send a telegram to the National Assembly to resolve to prosper the Beiping plan. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. (4th dispatch)

(Tianjin) People from all walks of life held a celebration assembly for the opening of the National Assembly at the public sports ground at 10:00 AM on the 5th. Due to rain, only 5,000 to 6,000 people attended. Officials from the provincial and municipal authorities and various departments and bureaus participated. Wang Shuchang, the chairman, reported the significance of the celebration. Zhang Xueming, Wang Yuke, Liu Chenzhang, and others all gave speeches and passed proposals to request the National Assembly to abolish unequal treaties and abolish consular jurisdiction. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. (5th dispatch) (Taiyuan) On the morning of the 5th, people from all walks of life in Taiyuan held a celebration assembly for the National Assembly at Zhongshan Park. More than 5,000 people attended. All private schools were closed to participate. Liang Xianda, the chairman, passed a telegram congratulating the opening of the National Assembly, requesting the People's Congress to resolutely abolish unequal treaties by revolutionary means, requesting the central government to restore financial public debt to raise military salaries for the stationed troops in Shanxi, and proposing to transfer stationed troops to suppress bandits and cultivate land. Various recreational activities were not held due to rain and will be postponed to the expanded propaganda week on the 7th. (5th dispatch)

(Bengbu) People from all walks of life held a meeting at New World to celebrate the National Assembly. The entire city flew flags. The authorities strictly guarded against reactionaries due to the opening of the National Assembly. (5th dispatch)

(Xuzhou) On the morning of the 5th, people from all walks of life celebrated the opening of the National Assembly and the May 5th Memorial Day at the People's Education Hall. Recreational activities were held at noon. The entire city closed for one day to celebrate. (5th dispatch)

(Anqing) People from all walks of life held a celebration assembly for the National Assembly at the Huangjia drill ground at 9:00 AM on the 5th. Recreational activities were held in the afternoon and evening. (5th dispatch)

(Jinan) Today, the entire city flew flags and streamers. All government agencies and schools were closed. A celebration assembly was held at the city government, and lights were hung in the evening. (5th dispatch)

(Harbin) Today, all agencies celebrated the Double Fifth Festival. A celebration was held at the Governor's Office at 10:00 AM. Businesses flew flags and streamers. All newspapers issued special editions and stopped publication for one day. (5th dispatch) (Qingjiangpu) Huaiyin celebrated the May 5th Memorial Day and the opening of the National Assembly. All took a day off, and lantern parades were held in the evening to express their celebration. (5th dispatch)

Situation of Legal Rights Negotiations 24

Denmark, Sweden and Other Countries Intend to Abandon

(Beiping) The mission has suspended legal rights negotiations. Since our country has announced a standstill, many countries have gradually softened their attitude due to public opinion. Countries such as Denmark, Sweden, Portugal, Brazil, Norway, and Cuba, although using the attitude of the major powers as a benchmark, have secretly expressed their intention to abandon and are preparing to abandon before countries such as England, America, and France. (5th dispatch)

(Nanjing) The British and French envoys returned north one after another within days. (5th dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Japanese side has made some claims regarding the regulations for the management of foreigners. (5th dispatch)

Hu Hanmin Visited Friends Yesterday 25

(Nanjing) Hu Hanmin came out to visit friends at 11:00 AM this morning and then returned to his residence. (5th dispatch)

He Jian Departs for the Capital 26

(Nanjing) He Jian telegraphed that he had departed from Changsha and would arrive within two days. (5th dispatch)

(Changsha) The Xiang Army has been in arrears with military pay for more than four months. The various army and division management offices requested He Jian to convene a meeting of the various division commanders to dismiss the unarmed and redundant personnel and unify the military education institutions. (4th dispatch)

Wang Chonghui Wants to Go to Europe 27

(Nanjing) Wang Chonghui told visitors that he hopes to work for the government as a judge at The Hague. Those who tried to dissuade him asked Wang to return to the capital first and wait for the end of the National Assembly before going to the International Court of Justice. (5th dispatch)

Wang Boqun is Ill 28

(Nanjing) Wang Boqun was indeed in bed when he met Yu Feipeng the day before yesterday. He said that he had intended to come to the capital despite his illness, but the doctor advised him not to move due to fever and chills. He Yingqin had telegraphed him urgently, no matter what, he must come to the capital. Wang also entrusted Yu to bring the original draft of his telegram to He to the capital for review. He brought his family to the capital last night. (5th dispatch)

The Situation in Guangdong Eases 29

(Nanjing) According to the reconnaissance report from the Xiang and Gan aircraft here, the situation in Guangdong is not as serious as advertised in the telegrams and by the reactionaries. Moreover, a part of the Red bandits has collapsed towards the Fujian border. Key figures are optimistic about the current situation. (5th dispatch)

Explosion at a Guangdong Powder Magazine 30

(Hong Kong) At 7:30 AM on the 5th, an explosion occurred at the powder magazine of the Zhongliudi Pillar Fortress, injuring more than ten people and killing several. (5th dispatch)

The Gang Bandits Collapsed Westward 31

(Nanjing) The bandit situation in Jiangxi has changed recently, and they have collapsed westward. The 5th Brigade of the 28th Division is currently stationed in Gupingxu, attacking Beishixu in Beibei. The newly arrived bandits are being led by Gong Bingfan, the commander of the division, with his direct troops and the Yang regiment stationed in Daijiafang. Chai Brigade is advancing to suppress the area around Loutilin and Dahu, killing more than a hundred bandits. They are joining forces with various troops to encircle them. (5th dispatch)

(Changsha) He Yingqin telegraphed that the Gan bandits are moving westward, urging preparations to meet them head-on. Yuan Ying's troops have been transferred to Puqi. (4th dispatch)

Yu Xuezhong Talks About the Recent Situation of the Troops 32

(Beiping) At 6:00 PM today, reporters met Yu Xuezhong in Zhongshan Park. According to him, the six brigades under his command are stationed in the Zhangyuan and Baoding areas, intensifying training. Military pay for February has been fully paid, with the same treatment as all the troops in the Northeast. (5th dispatch)

(Beiping) Military police caused trouble at the Chengnan Amusement Park a few days ago. Yu Xuezhong went to the park yesterday in plain clothes with his family to inquire about the cause of the incident from the vendors in the park under the pretext of watching a play. He left the park and instructed the military police authorities to severely punish the perpetrators. (5th dispatch)

Northeast Permits the Issuance of Military Uniforms for Pang and Song's Troops 33

(Beiping) Pang Bingxun told reporters that the Northeast has agreed to issue 50,000 sets of military uniforms to Song Zheyuan, Sun Dianying, and my troops. They have been allocated and are waiting for train loading in Tianjin. My headquarters will receive a total of 7,500 sets according to the number of people. I will bring the military uniforms back to the defense area as soon as a sum of money is raised. Soldiers take obedience as their duty. I absolutely obey the deputy commander and support peace and unity. I hope the Communist bandits will be eliminated as soon as possible. (5th dispatch)

Strange News of a Black Donkey Filing a Complaint 34

(Beiping) A strange news story of a black donkey filing a complaint has occurred here. Liu Deshan, a farmer in Jinzhan Village, Sunjiang Town, Pingbei, was riding a black donkey through Guangcun last winter when he was suddenly robbed by bandits who killed Liu and robbed his property. The black donkey escaped. The case has not been solved for a long time. Yesterday, a young and strong man was riding a black donkey through Jinzhan Village. After the donkey entered the village, it neighed and jumped and broke into the home of Liu Deshan, the deceased. The Liu family saw that the donkey belonged to their family and invited the village chief and others to capture the strong man and send him to the Daxing Public Security Bureau for strict interrogation. The criminal was arrested and is awaiting interrogation. (5th dispatch)

The Little Entente Authorities Hold Secret Deliberations 46

French Prime Minister Criticizes Tax Treaty Remarks

Causing Consistent Indignation in German Public Opinion

National Press, Rome, 4th - The foreign ministers of the Little Entente are currently holding secret deliberations in Rome, while King Carol of Romania and the Yugoslavian Head of State Alexander suddenly met on the banks of the Danube in Wasuva. The prime ministers of both countries were also present. The matters discussed are unknown because no news has been released and both parties have maintained strict secrecy. According to another report, the two heads of state discussed the German-Austrian tax treaty and France's counterproposal.

National Press, Berlin, 4th - French Prime Minister Laval's speech on Sunday in Connaught, mentioning the German-Austrian tax treaty and saying that France would hardly tolerate it, has caused indignation in German public opinion. The most extreme faction even stated that Germany should change its diplomatic policy as soon as possible and immediately withdraw from the League of Nations. Other newspapers that have always advocated German-French friendship, such as the Berliner Tageblatt, also expressed opposition to Laval's remarks. Even the Germania newspaper, which is peaceful and related to Prime Minister Bruning, stated that Laval's remarks were roughly the same as those of Briand and other French politicians, all groundless accusations. It is suspected that France's psychology is simply that the German-Austrian tax treaty was not approved by France in advance, so it is regarded as detrimental to France's dignity. If that is the case, then France is acting as the master of Europe. In the future, if a sparrow falls from the roof without the prior consent of the French Foreign Ministry, the French can consider it to be related to France's dignity. According to the Germania newspaper's tone, which has always been peaceful, even it is now using strong words, which shows that the French people's arbitrary attacks on an ordinary economic integration have reached an unbearable point.

International Chamber of Commerce Conference 47

The Scope of the Agenda is Broad

Disputes Are Inevitable

Reuters, Washington, 4th - The International Chamber of Commerce opened its conference today, attended by 1,000 representatives from 47 countries. President Hoover delivered a welcoming speech, urging people in the business community to promote disarmament, as disarmament is the most effective way to restore economic prosperity, which cannot be achieved by any other means. The conference organizers expect this conference to have good results, but the scope of the agenda is broad and disputes may be inevitable. Associated Press, Washington, 4th - The Chinese Committee of the International Chamber of Commerce submitted a statement to the conference today, requesting active support and immediate convening of an international silver conference, claiming that China is the world's largest user of silver and is prepared to participate in the conference to jointly plan methods to increase and stabilize silver prices.

Associated Press, Washington, 4th - The president of the Japanese shipping company stated in his speech at the International Chamber of Commerce conference today that there are many serious commercial problems in the Far East, involving China and the difficulty of trade with China after the fall in silver prices, but solving silver prices must be done by China itself, because the cause of the price drop does not provide a basis for external forces to provide relief.

Spain Prepares for Parliamentary Elections 48

To Deal with the Catalan Autonomy Movement

Consensus Growing Within the Government

The Interior Minister's Resignation Has Been Withdrawn

The Anarchist Party is Becoming Active

National, Madrid, 5th - The Spanish government has decided to temporarily shelve the issue of allowing the Russian Trotsky to reside in Spain, leaving it to the first Republican government after the election of parliament to resolve. Regarding the central government's attitude towards the Catalan autonomy movement, opinions among cabinet members are gradually converging. Interior Minister Mora has agreed to withdraw his resignation. According to his plan, the number of seats in parliament will be increased from 410 to 600. The country will be divided into 50 districts, with one representative for every 40,000 voters, in order to correct the past imbalance in urban and rural representation.

National Press, Madrid, 4th - Interior Minister Mora suddenly resigned due to disagreements with Prime Minister Zamora over Catalonia. Mora told people that the Prime Minister was too lenient towards the Catalan separatists and lacked decisiveness. At the beginning of the new Republican government, this kind of government is extremely dangerous. At the same time, the domestic anarchist party believes that the establishment of the Republican government is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. Barcelona has long been a nest of anarchists, and it is not difficult to take it as a basis for development. Therefore, many flyers are found there every day, inciting the people to quickly rise up, rob the police of their guns, divide the land of the monasteries, and throw the people in the monasteries into the sea. Many anarchists have been arrested there. The central government and the Catalan local authorities have decided to strictly crack down on this kind of illegal activity.

British Chancellor of the Exchequer Proposes Land Tax 49

Starting with Estimated Land Prices

The Conservative Party Remains Silent for Now

Reuters, London, 4th - Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden outlined the land tax proposal in the House of Commons today and will present a finance bill, saying that he plans to levy a land tax starting from the 1933 fiscal year, levying one penny per pound per year. Agricultural land will not be taxed, but land prices exceeding agricultural land prices will be taxed. Land used for religious and charitable purposes, cemeteries, city-owned railroads, and public utilities will be exempt from tax. Those with land tax due not exceeding ten shillings will be exempt from tax. The estimation of land prices will begin in October this year and is expected to be completed within two years. The total cost of estimating land prices is estimated to be approximately 1 million to 1.5 million pounds. The method should be simple and direct to avoid disputes. The estimated value will be published to the public and may be used as a basis for the government to collect land and provide compensation and for local areas to collect donations in the future. Conservative Party leaders did not criticize this proposal much and will discuss it when they see the full text of the proposal. Chamberlain said that this tax will make landowners pay another income tax.

It is currently only aware that the negotiations have reached a stalemate. One of the difficulties is the issue of retained areas in Hankou, Guangzhou, Shanghai, and Tianjin. The House of Commons also inquired about the extraterritoriality issue. The Foreign Secretary stated that he intended to address the issue of extraterritoriality on May 6th and would not discuss it today. Today, London speculated that the British cruiser HMS Vindictive had been specially dispatched to Nanjing, but the Admiralty and the Foreign Office both claimed to have no knowledge of the ship changing its usual schedule for a special mission. (Note: This ship came to China to replace other British ships and happened to be in Nanjing at the time, but was merely en route to Hankou according to the established schedule. British naval personnel in Shanghai stated that there were no special operations involving British ships in China.)

Central Party Headquarters Commemorates the Anniversary of the Premier's Inauguration as President 51

Wu Jingheng Reports on Past Events

At 7:30 AM on May 5th, the Central Party Headquarters held a commemoration of the 10th anniversary of the Premier's inauguration as Extraordinary President. The attendees included Central Committee members Chiang Kai-shek, Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, Wu Jingheng, Chu Minyi, Zhang Daofan, Miao Peicheng, Dai Fu-xian, Wang Bailing, Yu Youren, Enke Batu, Shao Yuanchong, Ding Weifen, Zhang Renjie, Chen Guofu, Yang Shuzhuang, Kexing'e, Ding Chaowu, He Yingqin, Song Ziwen, as well as guests from various agencies and all staff of the Party Headquarters, totaling over 600 people. Yu Youren presided over the meeting, which commenced with music and the performance of rituals. Wu Jingheng then reported on the past events surrounding the Premier's inauguration as Extraordinary President, stating briefly: “Today, May 5th, is the 10th anniversary of the Premier's inauguration as Extraordinary President. There were many grand events on that day. I will now speak about a minor detail: it was raining this morning, and it was also raining that morning. However, the people of Guangzhou celebrating the Premier's inauguration as Extraordinary President did not diminish their enthusiasm for the celebration at all due to the rain. On that morning, the number of people celebrating in Guangzhou was no less than tens of thousands. At that time, I was going to the Premier's office and was already crowded by the people in front of the Finance Department and could no longer move forward. Later, when I was about to go to France, the Premier summoned me and said that there were important things to discuss, which was to say that becoming the Extraordinary President was due to the various difficulties in the revolutionary and national salvation environment. The Northern Government had no value, and if there was no central construction in the government, the people would inevitably be disappointed. The Premier's inauguration as Extraordinary President was entirely due to the people's expectations. The Premier did not regard becoming President as a matter of glory, but rather as a matter of national salvation. He said that many of the people celebrating at that time did not hold the hope of being promoted or getting rich but were entirely driven by patriotic enthusiasm. Furthermore, when the Premier first took office as President of the Nanjing Government, I had just arrived in Shanghai from abroad and only came to Nanjing to see the Premier on January 4th. At that time, even though the Premier had taken office as President, he was still the same as usual. The room was still full of comrades, and everyone discussed state affairs as usual. The Premier said that becoming President was to cope with the environment, and the purpose was entirely for national salvation. The Premier suffered misfortune and went to Shanghai, and later returned to Guangdong. At that time, the environment was only for dealing with warlords and military affairs. The Premier was no longer determined to be President, and instead took the position of Grand Marshal and organized the Grand Marshal's Office in Guangzhou. The Premier's assumption of the positions of President and Grand Marshal were all due to the environmental needs for national salvation. The Premier did not regard the positions of President and Grand Marshal as a matter of course and always kept them in mind. Therefore, in the first year of the Republic of China, he did not regard the transfer of the Presidency to Yuan Shikai as a matter of course. However, because Yuan Shikai wanted to be emperor after becoming President, the Premier had to rise up again to oppose Yuan for national salvation. The Premier was not afraid of thousands of difficulties and setbacks in saving the country and always wanted to achieve the goal of saving China and achieving freedom and equality for China. The Premier told us that the few things that could not be forgotten the most were the few things that were solemnly entrusted to comrades. What are these few things? They are the last few words on the will (the recent proposals to convene a National Assembly and abolish unequal treaties must be realized in the shortest possible time). This is what should be done after unification and is no longer a problem. Also, the two sentences (the revolution has not yet succeeded, comrades still need to work hard) include everything that we should work hard to do. The opening ceremony of the National Assembly is held on today's May 5th anniversary, which has great significance. The people's celebration of the National Assembly today is also extraordinary. These are all the spirits of the Premier in heaven, as if above him, as if on his left and right, constantly monitoring us and helping us to achieve these good phenomena. My last wish is still the Premier's two sentences (the revolution has not yet succeeded, comrades still need to work hard), and I hope that comrades must work together. This is the meaning of today's commemoration.)” After the speech, the ceremony was completed and the meeting adjourned.

Guangdong Central Bank Announces Suspension of Cash Redemption 52

Value of Central Bank Notes Drops to 80%

Suspension of Tax Collection Also Announced for May

Guangzhou Correspondence – Since the Guangdong Provincial Central Bank experienced a run on April 27th, the number of people redeeming cash has been increasing daily. Until April 30th, rumors suddenly arose, and people became panicked. Therefore, on that day, the Central Bank and its Yonghan Road branch and Xidi office redeemed over ten thousand in cash. On that day, redemption was limited. Those with a small number of Central Bank notes, less than 100 yuan, could redeem them immediately, while those with several hundred to thousands of yuan were restricted. However, the Central Bank and its branch offices always had several hundred people from morning till evening, and they only dispersed after the suspension of redemption in the evening. Furthermore, the Jiangmen branch also experienced a run in recent days, redeeming about ten thousand in cash each day. As a result, the value of Central Bank notes continued to decline. When purchasing Hong Kong dollars with Central Bank notes, a discount of 650 yuan per thousand yuan was required. Some unofficial exchanges valued Central Bank notes at about 80% of cash value. The authorities were still concerned that the Central Bank would suffer a more severe run due to the influence of the situation, so they planned to temporarily announce the suspension of Central Bank redemption at an appropriate time to maintain the Central Bank's funds. The Central Bank notes that were discounted were to be bought and sold on the market. On May 1st, after Deng Zeru, Gu Yingfen, Lin Sen, and Xiao Focheng issued their telegram, the Central Bank also issued a notice of suspension of redemption, stating: "Now, by order of the Eighth Route Commander, with rumors rampant and people shaken, the Bank's banknotes are declining daily and are difficult to maintain. It is ordered that redemption be temporarily suspended from May 1st to await reorganization. Please comply accordingly, etc. This order is hereby notified to all branches, which shall comply immediately. This notice is given separately. (Director Shen Zaihe, Deputy Director Yang Jianping)" After the Central Bank suspended redemption, all branches also ceased redemption. As for all tax revenues of the Finance Department related to April, Central Bank notes are still accepted. Tax revenues for May will be temporarily suspended. It is rumored that a new method of paying taxes will be formulated. (May 1st)

Jinan Residents Hold May 3rd Memorial Service 53

Vow to Avenge Martyred Compatriots

Japanese Residents in Jinan Close Their Doors and Do Not Venture Out

Jinan Correspondence – The May 3rd Massacre is a great shame and humiliation for our country. From May 3, 1928, to today, three years have passed in the blink of an eye. The people of Jinan, suffering deep pain, are particularly heartbroken and indignant. This year, the May Revolution Memorial Day Preparatory Committee made early preparations to hold a memorial meeting for the third anniversary of the May 3rd Massacre at the Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters on the 3rd. Notices were issued to various agencies, schools, and businesses to fly flags at half-mast and close for one day. Slogans were posted throughout the city and suburbs. The Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters, Licheng County Party Headquarters, and May Revolution Memorial Day Preparatory Committee all published proclamations to the people to alert the public. On this day, the Shandong Executive Department of the Korean Great Independence Party also distributed a letter to Chinese comrades to commemorate the May 3rd Massacre in China. The atmosphere in the city suddenly became tense, and the people expressed deep sorrow. As for the opening of the memorial meeting, from 9:00 AM, more than a thousand representatives from all walks of life gathered in the auditorium of the Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters for the meeting. In the center of the auditorium was set up the spiritual tablet of the martyrs of the May 3rd Massacre. The chairman of the Shandong Provincial Rectification Committee, Zhang Weicun, presided over the meeting. Then, mournful music was played, and all bowed three times to the national flag, the Premier's portrait, and the spiritual tablets of Cai Gongshi and the martyrs of the May 3rd. Flower wreaths were offered, and a memorial text was read. The chairman then reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating briefly: "On this day in 1928, many revolutionary armed forces and volunteers were massacred by Japanese imperialists in an inhumane manner, which is most distressing. Japan dreamed of using force to achieve its ambitions of aggression. Zhang Zongchang wanted to use foreign forces to maintain his power, and they colluded with each other, thus causing this massacre. This is not only an unprecedented humiliation for our country but also a rare tragedy in the world. Today, we are holding the third anniversary memorial meeting. Everyone must work together to wash away the shame and prevent the recurrence of collusion between warlords and imperialists. I still remember that in 1928, Japanese imperialists could not stop the Northern Expedition of the Revolutionary Army. Now that the foundation of the Party and the country is solid, as long as the people of the country are not pessimistic and negative, then in the near future, we can defeat all the dreams of imperialists and wash away the shame of the May 3rd Massacre." Then, Wang Fangting, the director of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, Wu Zhenzan, the president of the Shandong High Court, Zhang Hongjian, the head of the Provincial Rectification Committee, and Wang Xiangrong, the director of the Department of Finance, gave speeches. At 10:30 AM, slogans were shouted, and photographs were taken before the meeting adjourned. The slogans of the meeting were: "Never forget the great shame and humiliation of May 3rd, rigorously implement economic severance with Japan, abolish all unequal treaties, supervise the government to rigorously implement revolutionary diplomacy, overthrow Japanese imperialism, vow to avenge the martyred compatriots of May 3rd, complete the National Revolution, Long live the Chinese Kuomintang, Long live the liberation of the Chinese nation." Furthermore, the Japanese Consul in Jinan, Nishida Koichi, had instructed Japanese residents in Jinan not to go out on the 3rd to avoid accidents. The Japanese residents also told each other to close their doors and not venture into the streets. Therefore, there were no traces of Japanese on the market on that day. (Month 3rd)

Supervisory Yuan Investigates Anhui Rice Public Bonds 54

Sends Councilor Shang Wenli to Wuhu

Wuhu Correspondence – Supervisory Yuan Councilor Shang Wenli arrived in Wuhu on the 3rd by order from Beijing to investigate whether taxes and levies were being collected under false pretenses after the abolition of likin. On the 4th, Mr. Shang personally consulted with the County Chamber of Commerce and various agencies on all matters. According to Mr. Shang's statement, “The Anhui Province's current borrowing of one million yuan in rice public bonds, according to the Chamber of Commerce, is for construction purposes and does not harm people's livelihoods, so it can be carried out. However, public bonds cannot be raised by levying rice taxes. As for the five inland regular customs, according to the general outline for the implementation of likin abolition, they should have been abolished by the end of November of last year. The reason why the Wuhu Regular Customs has not been abolished is that the plan has not yet been fully detailed. It is planned to investigate in detail and then submit it to the Executive Yuan for approval. I will stay in Wuhu for about three or four days. Once completed, I will go to Anqing, Datong, Tunxi, and other places to investigate.” (4th)

Local Correspondence

Jinshan 55

The bandits in southern Jinshan are rampant again. The banditry in Jinshan temporarily subsided after the execution of the bandit leaders Taibao Ashu, Zhudu, and Amei, but along the coast from Jinshanwei to Fuwangdai, the bandit leader Lu Yaosheng's subordinates still number in the hundreds and have not been eliminated. In recent days, the families of Monk Nan Yang in Fuwangdai, Tan Liuxian in northeast Jinshanwei, and Hou Zijian in Xinqiaotou have been robbed, losing hundreds of silver dollars and clothing.

Fengxian 56

Due to a clash during an arrest of gamblers by the Fengsong police team, Patrol Captain Zhang Yufang of the Public Security Bureau was ordered yesterday to go to Hujiaqiao to arrest gamblers. He arrested thirteen gamblers in the Xinxin Tea Garden in the town. While escorting them in batches, the Songjiang County Police First Squad stationed there came out to obstruct, causing a conflict, resulting in serious injuries to the Patrol Captain and others. He immediately went to the county overnight to report the incident. The chief of the sub-bureau, Zhu Huaiyi, approached the head of the Zhu sub-squad to negotiate, but without result. The county government has now requested the Songjiang County to thoroughly investigate the situation and has sealed up the Xinxin Tea Garden for investigation.

Wuxi 57

Zhang Yongqing commits suicide due to economic pressure. Zhang Yongqing, 47 years old, of the Huachang Cloth Store on the Yutou River along the Huangniqiao outside the North Gate of this county, has been experiencing sluggish business in recent years, leading to increasing financial difficulties. The other day, he was stimulated by economic problems and conceived the idea of suicide. He immediately went out alone to a pharmacy and bought two bottles of "Florida" calming pills and took fifteen pills alone when going to bed at night to die. The next day, his son Zuyin pushed the door open and went in to comfort his father and saw his face pale and unconscious, knowing that he had taken poison. He immediately took him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. According to Dr. Zhu, the poisoning was mild and there was no danger to his life.

The police team kills the bandit leader. Zhou Jiashan, the director of the Eighth Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau of this county, captured a bandit named Zhu Genda a few days ago in Yuanfu Bay, Zhoutanqiao, Xin'an Township. After interrogation, he was transferred to the county government. Magistrate Pan Xun personally interrogated the suspect in court. The suspect confessed in court that the bandit leader Hang Zubei was now hiding in the home of the Mud Bridge in Junzhang Mountain, Nanfangquan, Kaihua Township, in the 14th District, etc. After Magistrate Pan obtained the confession, he secretly ordered the police captain Wang Wei to send a special agent Wang Jinbiao to lead five team members to the countryside to arrest the bandit leader Hang Zubei and his two accomplices. Upon seeing the detectives arrive, they dared to open fire and resist arrest. The special agents also returned fire and shot the bandit Hang in the left shoulder and leg, causing him to fall to the ground and die. The remaining two bandits, seeing the situation was not good, fled in succession. Afterwards, Special Agent Wang reported to Captain Wang Wei by telephone. Captain Wang Wei hired an open boat at 9:00 AM yesterday (5th) and transported the body of the slain bandit leader Hang Zubei to the boat. It was towed by a steamship to the city and docked under the Gongyun Bridge. Captain Wang reported to the county government. Magistrate Pan reported to the county court and requested that personnel be sent to verify the identity.

Jiangyin 58

Villagers in Lishan Township brutally murdered by bandits. Jiang Longda and Jiang Sanda, brothers and villagers in Lishan Township in the Sixth District, usually harbored enmity towards bandits and assisted the authorities in detaining them, leading to resentment from the bandits. They had fled to other places to avoid them. The other day, Longda returned home for business and was detected by bandits on the first day at about 8:00 PM. He was brutally murdered by the bandits, and his head was cut off and thrown into a wheat field. On the 2nd, County Magistrate Li went to the countryside to inspect the work of cleaning up bandits. Upon hearing the report from the Sixth District Office, he personally went to inspect. The 　Tangqiao was robbed and injured. On the night of the 2nd, the Su family in Huangtangqiao outside the East Gate was robbed, and the owner and his wife were injured by bullets. The owner was shot in the arm, and his wife was shot in the abdomen, endangering her life. They were taken to the Gospel Hospital for treatment that night.

Gaoyou 59

A nine-year-old child commits suicide by poisoning. Chen Jiuyu's son, nicknamed Xiaogouzi, a farmer from Chenjiaxia in the county, is nine years old this year. The other day, he quarreled with a neighboring child, which caused his mother to scold him severely. Unexpectedly, Xiaogouzi, in a fit of anger, secretly took fire matches and burned alcohol and swallowed it. By the time his family noticed, it was too late to save him. It is said to be tragic.

Jurong 60

Provincial Security Team engages in fierce battle with bandits. Yu Shimei, the commander of the Fourth Battalion of the Third Regiment of the Provincial Security Team stationed in Xiashu Town to suppress bandits, learned at the end of last month that 60 to 70 bandits were entrenched in the Zhengpan Mountain of Cangtou Town. He immediately sent a team to encircle and suppress them. Unexpectedly, they encountered each other on the way, and the two sides engaged in a fierce battle for about three hours. The bandits could not resist and fled to the southwest Huashan. The team then tracked and pursued them. As a result, Company Deputy Yang Tao was wounded, and Huang Mingyue, a team soldier, was injured. Three hostages, Wang Zhiren and others, were rescued. The bandit leader Liang Laoda was killed, and bandits Wu Qishu, Tang Dayu, Ting Tang Guantai, and Yuan Fangrang were captured alive.

Shangyu 61

A cotton boat encounters thieves midway. Han Hongsheng from Pudong, Shanghai, opened the Hongji Flower Shop in Songsha Town, Weixi, specializing in purchasing cotton for various flower factories in Shanghai. This time, he purchased more than 500 bales of pure white flowers. The other day, he loaded them onto a sea boat from Tancun in the town to Shen. As soon as the boat sailed out of the back sea, it suddenly encountered a pirate boat, which robbed it. At the same time, a boat of live pigs from the north of the sea was also robbed. After the pig boat owner reported it, the Yongping warship, which was patrolling, opened its engines to pursue. They encountered each other in the Taizhou waters, and the two sides opened fire. As a result, the bandits were no match and abandoned the flower boat. The boat was then taken to Haimen by the Yongping warship. After the owner Han Hongsheng learned of this, he rushed to collect it and requested that the original ship escort it to Shanghai. The loss of goods in this battle was more than 2,000 gold.

The wife of a prisoner in jail is in love with someone else. Wang Chengcai, a police officer from the Qianbaiguan Public Security Bureau, was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment by the county last year for sheltering opium gambling. He was released from prison a few days ago and returned home. He then realized that his wife's temperament had changed drastically, as if she were a different person. He became suspicious and later learned that his wife had become acquainted with someone during his imprisonment. Wang was furious and turned to question his wife. Unexpectedly, his wife retorted. Wang was short-tempered and secretly swallowed opium paste to commit suicide. Fortunately, neighbors managed to rescue him. While the chaos was happening, his wife escaped to the Lianghu lover's house. It is said that Wang went to find him after waking up.

Xiaoshan 62

Brothers misunderstand each other and perish together. Feng, brothers of the same clan in Luomenzhen, southern Xiaoshan, were always on good terms. On the night of the 30th of last month, Yaotian was picking leaves in the mulberry garden, and Zhitian suspected him of being a thief and used a hoe to strike him, smashing Yaotian's head and spilling his brains, killing him on the spot. Zhitian knew that he had caused a disaster and jumped into the West Xiaojiang to commit suicide. The next morning, the two corpses were seen by neighbors, who investigated the truth and realized the truth. They have already been buried separately.

Pinghu 63

The Dengying Primary School is set on fire. Since the principal of Dengying Primary School in the city, Xu Gengyu, ran away and disappeared, the Education Bureau has appointed Feng Fukui as an agent for several months, and things have been fine. Unexpectedly, someone set a fire at the back door the other night (3rd). By the time they noticed, the fire was raging, and the back door was completely burned down. After Patrol Chief Shi of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau was notified, he rushed to the scene, but the arsonist had already escaped without a trace. He immediately ordered a strict investigation.

The county government limits the demolition of leaning houses. The County Public Security Bureau received instructions from the County Government, roughly stating that the houses on the north end of the Ganhe Street Meat Shop Lane to the Pingmin Daily Newspaper are leaning too much. The houses that are an eyesore and will affect public safety. The demolition and reconstruction of the houses should be notified in accordance with Article 17 of the County Construction Regulations to maintain public safety, and the compliance should be reported for inspection and verification. After receiving the order, the Public Security Bureau has notified the landlords to comply.

Ningbo 64

A Taiwanese bandit leader is caught. The bandit leader Zhan Meidong is from the West Township Street in Taizhou. His subordinates number in the hundreds and have been robbing in the Taizhou native place, causing much suffering to those who were poisoned.
