Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Anhui Silk Cocoon Association Petitioned the Government to Protect Cocoon Merchants 121

Chairman Huang Chen of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Anhui Silk Cocoon General Office Committee presented a document to the National Government yesterday, saying that the purpose of the presentation was to protect the cocoon market, prepare in advance, refer to the methods of previous years' petitions, and respectfully ask the government to review and approve the distribution of orders to the provincial governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui to strictly protect the cocoon-producing areas to ensure the safety of farmers and merchants. Because the cocoon production in the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui varies due to different times and geographical conditions, the cocoon market in each county opens at different times around the Lesser Fullness solar term. Ningbo and Shaoxing in Zhejiang are especially early. Over the years, the General Office has proposed and petitioned the three provincial governments to transfer orders for protection and print protection methods and present them to the military, county government, and public security bureaus in various places for reference and handling, so that the protection can be thorough and everyone is deeply grateful. This year's cocoon market has arrived, and the social situation is still peaceful. However, the brigands in various rural areas have not been put down, and the cocoon-producing areas in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are all located in waterways for transportation. During the cocoon season, silver and goods are exchanged. Without sending troops to patrol and protect along the way, it is not enough to prevent unforeseen events. As for Anhui Province, the journey is farther and the local security is not comparable to that of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The protection of each cocoon-producing area is even more important. Most of the cocoon merchants in each province are located in rural towns, and the protection force is not as strong as that of cities. The safety of farmers carrying cocoons to the merchants and cocoon merchants carrying banknotes to the merchants to collect cocoons is of great importance. The routes passed or the locations of the firms must have the strength to maintain order so that fear can be avoided and incidents can be quelled. The General Office's responsibility lies in preparing for the worst and noting the matters that should be protected, such as the loading and transportation of silver dollars and the transportation of dry cocoons, with reference to the usual situation, noting the date in each article, and respectfully requesting the government to preside over the handling and distribute orders to the three provincial governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui before the deadline to quickly order the stationed troops and the governments of various counties and the water and land public security bureaus to protect them in accordance with the regulations and implement them in an integrated manner, and the General Office will present copies of the methods and articles to the three provincial governments for distribution to the cocoon-producing areas for reference and handling, and all matters related to the early petition for protection of the cocoon market are attached with the methods for review and filing by the government and for separate implementation and begging for the command to comply with the above for the sake of public convenience, and respectfully presenting them to the National Government (the articles on protecting the cocoon market are omitted)

Shanghai Silk Reeling Industry Union Petitioned for Mediation 122

Discounted Wages Are Only Heard of in the National Industry

Silk Prices Have Risen but Wages Have Not Been Restored to Original Levels

The Shanghai Yinxiang District and Zhabei District Second Silk Reeling Industry Union has repeatedly requested the factory to restore the original wages in order to maintain a livelihood because life is becoming more difficult and silk prices have risen, but the factory has not responded. Yesterday, it jointly petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation. The content of its petition is as follows: (1) Number of workers related to the dispute: 9,000 female workers, 900 male workers, and 3,500 child workers in the Fourth District (i.e., Yinxiang District); 30,000 female workers, 2,700 male workers, and 15,000 child workers in the Sixth District (i.e., Zhabei District). (2) The main point of the dispute is to request the guild to notify each factory to restore all wages for male and female workers to the original amount starting from May 1st (Reason) In November last year, the silk reeling industry workers, in order to forgive the factory's difficult business, adopted the principle of mutual assistance and understanding between labor and capital to seek industrial development, and did not hesitate to sacrifice pain to temporarily calculate wages at 85% of the original amount. Since the wage reduction, gold prices have continued to rise and prices have skyrocketed. The cost of living has continued to increase. To this day, the wages of workers who work hard all day long not only cannot take care of a family, but also cannot afford their own basic food and clothing. If this continues, the workers will be waiting to die. Moreover, now that silk prices have risen compared to last winter, reaching more than 1,000 taels in February this year, the factory has not automatically restored wages at this time, ignoring the suffering of the workers. The urgency of the workers is as described above. The restoration of the original wage amount is really urgent to temporarily extend the lives of these tens of thousands of workers. Moreover, the wage reduction was originally temporary and has now been half a year, so it cannot be said to be temporary. Moreover, wage reduction is not only rare in all industries in Shanghai, but also only heard of in all industries in the country. Under these circumstances, the factory should not delay any longer for reasons. The meaning is clear (3) The course of the dispute On April 1st of this year, workers from various silk factories in Xinzha, Sixth District, went on strike due to the fact that wages should not only not be reduced but should be increased in Shanghai, where the cost of living is increasing. Later, the bureau sent people to persuade and agreed to find a way to mediate so that the factory would restore the original wage amount. The workers followed the orders of their superiors and immediately returned to work. Today, a month has passed, and there is still no news of restoration. The panic of the workers has reached its peak. Recently, the association and others have repeatedly received complaints from workers about the difficult living conditions, crying and crying. Therefore, on the 25th and 26th of last month, the association and others sent letters to the guild, relaying the plight of the workers, requesting that the guild notify each factory to restore wages to the original amount starting from May 1st. Unexpectedly, ten days have passed and the guild has ignored it. The workers in the two districts are worried and angry. The association and others have no choice but to petition for mediation in order to achieve the goal so that the workers can work hard at production with peace of mind and avoid accidents. Therefore, I urge you to mediate fairly and urgently.

Various Industries Request Reduction in Business Tax 124

Western Clothing Industry: The Shanghai Western Clothing Trade Association has submitted petitions to the Municipal Government and Finance Bureau regarding business tax issues. It is reported that the association's members, due to the high tax rates being unbearable, recently submitted a supplementary statement of opinions to the Municipal Government and Finance Bureau. An excerpt of the original text is as follows: "Submitted as a supplementary statement on business tax opinions, humbly requesting review and adoption to reduce the business tax rate for the Western clothing industry, alleviating the burden on businesses and sustaining people's livelihoods. Having previously read in the newspaper that (Your Honor) (Director of the Finance Bureau) has issued statements on the business tax issue, accommodating the opinions of merchants and residents as much as possible, our association previously presented our humble views on March 16 and dispatched Wang Lianfang and six others to meet with (Your Honor) (Director of the Finance Bureau), requesting consideration of the difficulties faced by businesses and a lenient drafting of the business tax rate for the Western clothing industry to sustain people's livelihoods. Unexpectedly, the April 20 newspaper reported that (The Municipal Government Finance Bureau) (Your Bureau) intends to set the draft business tax rate for Western clothing manufacturing at 20 per mille of capital, and for sales at 10 per mille of turnover, both at the highest rates. The clothing industry is taxed at 5 per mille of capital, while the garment industry is taxed at 2 per mille of turnover. The business tax rates for the same type of business are so disparate, which is contrary to Your Honor's principle of considering merchants and residents. Our Western clothing, as a type of clothing, is in the same category as robes and jackets, serving as the primary necessity for warmth and covering the body, and is universally used around the world. Article 4 of the national uniform system regulations also adopts it, and all military, political, industrial, commercial, and academic circles are happy to use it. It does not seem to be in the category of goods to be eliminated. Moreover, the price of domestically produced Western clothing is only about five or six yuan in national currency, while robes, jackets, and similar items made of silk or foreign goods cost no less than forty or fifty yuan. Therefore, Western clothing is not of a luxury nature. For example, if Western clothing manufacturers use Western methods and robe manufacturers use Chinese methods, they are both manufactured by Chinese people and are manual industries. Moreover, retailers of overcoats, cloaks, capes, and other clothing items are in the same business as Western clothing retailers. Therefore, the business tax rate for the Western clothing industry should be the same as that for the clothing manufacturing industry, and the sales industry should be taxed at 2 per mille, with no disproportionate burden imposed. Your Honor is knowledgeable about business conditions and widely gathers opinions from various industries. We hereby submit this document, humbly requesting review and adoption to reduce the business tax rate for the Western clothing industry to sustain people's livelihoods. This would be a great kindness."

Clock and Watch Industry: Since the Finance Bureau announced the draft business tax assessment standards and tax rate table for the city, the tax rate for the clock and watch industry is listed in the highest tier, alongside cosmetics. The preparatory committee of the industry's association believes that clocks and watches are daily necessities and that taxing them at the same rate as cosmetics is inappropriate. They convened an emergency meeting of the preparatory committee and decided to send letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various industry tax rule research committees, requesting them to forward a request to the Finance Bureau for a reduction. They also dispatched Zhuang Honggao, Chen Duomin, and Yan Boying to the business tax preparation office to appeal and submit a written statement expressing their firm resolve. An excerpt of the statement is as follows: "Submitted to humbly present the situation and request consideration. We have read in Announcement No. 1 from Your Office that the 'Regulations and Implementation Rules for the Collection of Business Tax in This City, as well as the Assessment Standards and Tax Rate Table, have been drafted by Your Office after inviting consultants, specialized commissioners, and others to deliberate and will be discussed with representatives from the Chamber of Commerce to ensure appropriateness. Business tax is a newly created tax, and thorough research is essential at the outset. If the various industry associations in this city have any opinions, they should be submitted to the Chamber of Commerce representatives for compilation or directly to Your Office for discussion within two weeks.' This shows Your Office's open-mindedness and extensive consultation. Our association's clock and watch industry has a tax rate of 20 per mille for manufacturers and 10 per mille for retailers. Clocks and watches are tools for measuring time and are essential for people's livelihoods. Individuals and organizations cannot maintain punctuality without clocks and watches, which would lead to chaos and instability in society. This is not an exaggeration. The work and rest schedules of various organizations, such as political, industrial, and commercial groups, are determined by a fixed time. Without clocks and watches to measure time, railway transportation would inevitably suffer repeated failures. Without clocks and watches, ocean-going steamships cannot know their speed and would be like blind people riding blind horses, creating dangerous situations. These are just a few major examples, and their close relationship with people's livelihoods is such that they cannot be dispensed with even for a day. Since clocks and watches are essential for people's livelihoods and their absence would affect social stability, even though most clocks and watches are imported, their importance is comparable to that of wages, rice, cloth, and silk. How can they be regarded as luxury goods simply because they are imported? If it is said that clocks and watches made of gold and silver should be classified as luxury goods, then the grades of rice are also numerous. In terms of the higher grades, they can also be regarded as luxury goods. Cosmetics are absolute luxury goods. The tax rate for our clocks and watches is the same as that for cosmetics. Comparing the cost of cosmetics with the cost of clocks and watches, it is self-evident which is heavier and which is lighter. The cost is so light, and the needs of people's livelihoods are so great. How can it be appropriate to levy the same tax on such different items? Since the need for clocks and watches is equal to that for wages, rice, cloth, and silk, whether manufacturing or selling, the tax rate should be the same as 1 per mille, which is fair. Therefore, we have prepared this detailed statement and humbly request your review and adoption to maintain people's livelihoods. This would be a public service. Respectfully submitted."

Cosmetics Industry: The Cosmetics Trade Association submitted a document to the Municipal Government and Finance Bureau the other day regarding the business tax issue, stating, "Submitted to request a reduction in the business tax rate for the cosmetics industry to benefit domestic products and maintain people's livelihoods. The April 20 newspaper reported that (The Municipal Government Finance Bureau) (Your Bureau) intends to set the draft business tax rate for the cosmetics industry at 20 per mille of capital for manufacturers and 10 per mille of turnover for retailers, both at the highest rates, causing widespread consternation. The unit price of domestically produced cosmetics is only a few cents or a few dimes, and their uses include dental care, skin care, relief of existing ailments, and promotion of health. They are daily necessities for personal hygiene, unlike imported cosmetics, which cost more than one yuan per unit and are used by wealthy families and those who indulge in luxury. Most imported cosmetics in our country are sold by Western medicine businesses or foreign goods businesses, so their business tax rate only needs to be paid once according to the Western medicine or foreign goods business rate. However, domestic cosmetics manufacturers never sell imported finished cosmetics, which is one proof that the cosmetics manufacturing industry in this city is purely operated by Chinese merchants. Therefore, the business tax rate is already levied on the factory as a manufacturer, on the distribution center as a wholesaler, and on the retail store as a retailer. Domestic cosmetics that have undergone three stages of taxation want to compete with imported cosmetics that are taxed only once. That is like climbing a tree to catch fish. Now, the government is actively promoting domestic goods and issuing clear orders to encourage industry. As recently reported, the Ministry of Industry has consulted the Ministry of Finance to exempt taxes on imitated foreign goods, stating that the raw materials used for these machine-made goods are mostly purchased from abroad and have already been taxed once upon import. It seems that taxes should not be levied again after the goods are manufactured to increase their burden. Moreover, many machine-made foreign goods are daily necessities for people's livelihoods. If the tax is too heavy, the cost will naturally increase, directly affecting the sales of domestic goods and indirectly encouraging the import of foreign goods. The principal and surcharges should be exempted to show encouragement and provide relief. Our domestically produced cosmetics are one of the items that should be exempt from taxes, and the business tax rate should also be leniently drafted so that domestic production can develop and recover lost profits. (The Finance Bureau) (Your Bureau) publishes the solicitation of opinions from various industries, and the intention is none other than this. We hereby submit this document, humbly requesting review and adoption (immediately order the Finance Bureau to) (allow) the business tax rate for the cosmetics industry to be taxed as daily necessities, generally at 2 per mille, to benefit domestic products and maintain people's livelihoods. This would be a great kindness." They also sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, saying, "Respectfully, we previously read in the newspaper that the Municipal Finance Bureau is collecting opinions from various industries for the business tax issue for discussion. Therefore, our association submitted a document to Mayor Zhang and Finance Bureau Director Hao on May 4 (same as above). However, we later heard that the Ministry of Finance's interpretation of the scope of business tax is that wholesalers who directly purchase from manufacturers can be exempted from taxation. However, the draft tax rate set by the municipal government is still higher than the regulations for the Western medicine industry and the foreign goods industry. Therefore, we request that Your Association forward the above-mentioned information to the five representatives attending the Finance Bureau meeting, considering the difficulties of our industry, and strive for our rights to alleviate our distress. We hope you will consider and reply with great anticipation."

Fish Industry: The Ice-Fresh Fish Trade Association recently submitted a statement of reasons and opinions to the various industry associations of the city's Tax Rule Research Committee, requesting a reduction in the tax rate for the fish industry, which the Municipal Finance Bureau intends to include in the 2 per mille tax category. The reasons stated in the opinion letter generally say that fish is a common food item and is especially needed by the general working class. Considering the current fish prices, the lower-priced ones sell for only about three or four yuan per load, which is actually cheaper than ordinary local vegetables. Moreover, ice-fresh fish are exposed to the dangers of wind and waves in the ocean during harvesting and transportation, and they are often robbed by pirates. The hardship and suffering are far greater than those of other industries. This should be taken into account when levying taxes, and special consideration should be given to reducing the tax burden. What should be especially noted is that in recent years, Japanese fishing boats have frequently crossed the border to fish, acting as the host and causing great aggression. Not only is the livelihood of fishermen becoming increasingly tight, but the fish industry is also gradually declining. The government of our country, aware of this, knows that it must be remedied as soon as possible. It has recently announced a clear order to exempt all fish taxes and fishery taxes, sincerely setting up ways to eliminate the impact of Japanese fishermen and to actively maintain and give preferential treatment to the fishing industry. Reducing their burden by one cent is to increase their vitality by one cent. In this way, the great effect can be achieved from the root. Therefore, the business tax of the fish industry should be changed to the 1 per mille category to be taxed, so that it can live up to the government's intention to promote it and make its revitalization hopeful. The future of the fish industry is very fortunate.

Pollen Industry: The Pollen Trade Association held a regular meeting yesterday, attended by Jiang Shouqi, Xu Furu, Song Yunji, Yang Housheng, Cao Liting, and others, to discuss business matters. It was resolved that, although there are no explicit regulations on how much to collect for this industry, those in charge may not fully understand the various difficulties involved. Therefore, it is necessary to state the facts and make a request. The original letter reads, "We are pleased that the comrades have been fighting legally to reach the goal of 2 per mille for the current business affairs in this city. We have exhausted our wisdom and spared no effort, and our association is especially grateful. We have something to ask. Although there are no explicit regulations on which category our pollen industry belongs to, we dare to briefly state the actual difficulties of our industry to avoid powder discrimination in the future. Our industry has a long history and is purely a national handcraft. After the intrusion of imported goods, it has plummeted and is in danger of extinction. Fortunately, the recent promotion of domestic goods has been revived slightly, otherwise it would have disappeared from the market long ago. However, the scale of business is very small, less than one-ten-thousandth compared with imports. It is difficult to survive with heavy taxes. In order to revive the national industry, we request that the comrades do their best to require that the business tax of our industry should not exceed 1 per mille to show the government's concern and to protect the business with a long history."

Xu Zhu, a Ningbo woman residing at No. 7, Sandeli, Fusantang Street, Xiaonanmen, Nanshi, aged 46, was walking to the street to buy vegetables in a basket around 9 am yesterday. "Marriage Problems in New China" is a Bestseller 129

The book "Marriage Problems in New China" was written by Mr. Lu Sihong based on the latest enacted Marriage Chapter of the Civil Code on Relatives, with reference to various current valid regulations and interpretations of precedents. The content is divided into six categories: (1) How to make an engagement; (2) How to dissolve an engagement; (3) How to get married; (4) How to form a family; (5) How to stipulate the marital property system; (6) How to divorce. The words are simple and the answers are detailed. In addition to the full text of the Marriage Chapter of the Civil Code on Relatives, the end of the book also includes the Central Political Conference's resolutions on the first points of the two chapters on relatives and inheritance in the Civil Code and the review opinions of its legal group. There are also Hu Hanmin's speech on legal equality between men and women and Fu Bingchang's speech on important issues in marriage legislation, which are excellent reference materials for readers. The book is prefaced by Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Cha Renwei, Pan Yangyao, and Yan Esheng. The price is only 80 cents. Since its publication, not only is the general distribution office, the Sanyi Bookstore at No. 17, Xintianxiang Lane, Beile Road, French Concession, packed, but also the various distribution offices, such as the Shijie Bookstore on Fourth Road, the Wenming Bookstore on Nanjing Road, and the publishing department of the Xinsheng Communications Agency in Dadaixinfang, Shilu East, Hankou Road, are also crowded.

Free Talk

World Little Things 138

— Sea Guest

London has newly discovered a school specializing in teaching wedding etiquette to general grooms and brides and new best men and ushers. All kinds of actions when getting married are carefully instructed, how to hold the bride's long skirt behind her, and how the bride should hold the groom's arm after the ceremony are all part of the curriculum.

New York has skyscrapers that are striking to the eye, but they are often demolished and rebuilt in less than fifteen or twenty years, not because the buildings are not strong, but because American businessmen like the latest office spaces. Therefore, the landlord can tear down and rebuild, and the cost of rebuilding is cheaper than having no tenants.

According to a famous British playwright, the nose and jaw are the most important parts of a woman's face in terms of beauty. If the nose and jaw are not beautiful, she cannot be considered a beauty.

Bullfighting and boxing are the most popular sports in Spain. Every time they are held, the whole country is in a frenzy, but the capital Madrid has a ban that children under the age of fourteen are not allowed to watch.

Everyone thinks that department stores were first created in the United States, but a professor at an American business school claims that the original founder was a British man, W. Whiteley, who established the first department store in London in 1863.

Two Successful People 139

— Jie Lu

If a person can set a goal, there is nothing that cannot be achieved. Once a goal is set, diligently develop resources, frugally manage expenses, treat people with humility and harmony, and examine oneself with an open mind. This is the path to success. In the past, someone offered the secret to getting rich to someone. A certain Mr. Jia used money to request this secret and received a piece of paper wrapped up. Upon opening it, it clearly read: "Diligence and Frugality," with no other secret. Although this is a playful story, it is a timeless saying. Ye Chengzhong, a boatman, and Yang Sisheng, a carpenter, both accumulated millions of assets through honesty, simplicity, diligence, and thrift. To this day, the Chengzhong Pudong and Second Schools stand tall on the Shanghai Bund, inspiring admiration. Some say that without luck and opportunity, one cannot succeed. If Ye Chengzhong had not encountered the Westerner who lost gold, and Yang Sisheng had not encountered the booming construction era, how could they have enjoyed such great fame? Therefore, luck and opportunity are bridges to success in life. However, from my own observation of these two individuals, there is no doubt that they embodied the ancient saying "seek much happiness for oneself." Why ask about luck and opportunity? One is Chen Baoshan, who collects old goods. Baoshan, from Wu, came to Shanghai alone fifteen years ago, carrying a basket and buying rags, glass bottles, and newspapers along the streets to make a living. He ate large pancakes and fried dough sticks to fill his stomach and slept in a garret at night, living the life of a garret dweller. In the morning, he scooped tap water to wash his face instead of using toiletries. He walked dozens of miles along the road every day, working tirelessly. After three years, he had some savings. He realized that there were no vendors selling earthenware jars and daily utensils along the streets, so he sold earthenware jars. He carried them on his shoulders, making a "dang dang" sound as he walked and shouted. Shanghai residents lived in small, cramped houses and often lacked utensils for storing things, so buyers flocked to him, and he made a considerable profit. Baoshan was humble and treated people with harmony, so wealthy families and large residences all knew him. Initially, he exchanged broken items for earthenware jars, and then, due to his honesty and trustworthiness, he gradually engaged in the trade of jewelry and precious stones. One day, he bought a pearl from a certain residence that was round like a bean and had a small handle. The owner reluctantly sold it to him for two taels of gold. Baoshan cut off the handle, and the pearl became perfectly round, white, and radiant. Later, he sold it to a Westerner for ten thousand taels of gold, and thus became wealthy. To this day, Baoshan travels to and from various wealthy families in Shanghai, buying and selling jewelry for the women. Even if the amount is tens of thousands of taels of gold, they trust him without any doubt. Baoshan himself said that when he had accumulated a hundred taels of silver, it was the most difficult time to manage. Small businesses were not worth it, and large businesses were not possible. At that time, he could not find a suitable business in his mind. The other is Fu A'san, who sells candy. A'san, from Yong, is blind in one eye. Foolishly, in Ning Shao Lun, I heard him talking about his success story with great interest. A'san said, "Twenty years ago, I was despised by others, so I held the ambition of 'I would rather not be an official than go to Xiangyang.' I came to Shanghai with one tael of silver and initially lived in a friend's house. Every day, I made a living by selling small candy ducks and chicken gizzards. When selling candy, I gave more or less depending on the wealth of the children. Rich children would often make a fuss if they saw poor children getting more. I would say, 'Your family has a lot of money and can buy more. He happened to get money, so I have to give him more.' Fortunately, young masters, please don't make a fuss. I loved reading novels such as 'Romance of the Three Kingdoms' and 'Water Margin' when I was young, and I was very familiar with them. Occasionally, I would tell stories to the children, and more and more people listened, and my business became more and more prosperous. After several years, I accumulated dozens of strings of cash, so I added children's toys and candies, pushing a cart as if it were a miniature children's treasury, traveling back and forth in the neighborhoods without interruption, rain or shine. Now that I am old, I have changed to opening a coal shop. This time, I took my son back to my hometown to sweep the tombs. After twenty years of struggle, I have finally achieved the goal of Fang Qing returning to Xiangyang."

A Record of Listening to Songs on a Spring Night 140

— Rui Hongchu

On the second day of the month, the Star Opera Troupe held its fifth rehearsal. I responded to Mr. Tang Jie's invitation and went with my colleague, Mr. Zhang Xueqin, to watch. The traffic on Route Doumer was heavy. When we entered the venue at eight o'clock, the gongs and drums were already sounding, and the performance had been going on for a long time. Ma Yin's and Wang Jiting's "Zhu Lian Village," Huang Yixuan's and Jing Liting's "Bao Lian Deng," Zhou Jianyun's and Ms. Liang Saizhen's "Mei Long Zhen," Zheng Zhengqiu's and Zheng Shihui's "Selling the Horse and Using the Iron Whip," Wang Xianzai's and Ms. Ying Yunwen's and Ying Shaomei's and Xie Yunqing's double performance of "Hong Luan Xi," Ms. Xuan Jinglin's and Wang Yushu's and Hong Zhen's "Fen He Bay," Ma Yin's and Dong Tianya's and Zhang Shichuan's and Zhou Jianyun's and Ms. Hu Die's and Wang Xianzai's and Tang Jie's and Jing Liting's "Dragon and Phoenix Auspicious," "Returning to Jingzhou," and "Lu Hua Dang." The costumes, stage movements, vocals, and acting of the above dramas were all extraordinary and much better than before. That night, there were no fewer than five hundred music lovers, and the seats were full. Those who arrived later shouted for more benches. Former movie star Ms. Zhang Zhiyun also shouted for more benches, creating a lively atmosphere. The Star Opera Troupe's special issue was distributed in the venue. Zhang Danweng wrote the preface and also composed a poem, saying: "Many years of mellow wine have cost me thought, the newspaper preface is for the rehearsal. Last month in Suzhou, I seemed to see from afar, an old friend strolling along the street. Vividly and skillfully, a marvelous female mimics a male. When Zhou Die takes the stage to perform 'Sitting in the Palace,' even though the prince consort shouts that it doesn't matter, he secretly worries about breaking the peony red." I returned late at night and jotted this down.

Also, Shi Weng's record of watching the Star Opera Troupe's fifth rehearsal said: "On May 2nd, I took my grand-nephew Baosen to watch. I felt that the stage was exquisite and the order was well-maintained. The male and female troupe members performed in turn, full of sound and color. Huang Yifeng's makeup in 'Cai Lou Pei' was beautiful, Gu Meijun's figure in 'Wu Long Yuan' was graceful like a willow in the wind, Xu Zhiren's demeanor in 'Si Lang Visits His Mother' was calm and composed, and Huang Lingxian's dignified and beautiful in 'Gan San Guan' was skilled in dancing. Zheng Zhengqiu in 'Huang He Lou' was generous and natural, and Zhou Jianyun's singing in 'Wu Jia Po' was absolutely beautiful. Su Wanjun's high-pitched singing was divine and wonderful. As for Dong Tianya in the play 'June Snow,' she was like an experienced grandmother, a true veteran. Gu Youmin's singing and dancing were like spring flowers, and Xuan Jinglin's sad songs were poignant and delicate, with natural charm everywhere, not forced. It can be said that she is excellent in both appearance and art."

Eight Million Pounds Sterling Nobody Wants 141

— Da Mei

A communication from London in April stated that the British Chancellor of the Exchequer had accumulated unclaimed funds over the years, which, with interest, now amounted to nearly eight million pounds sterling. The so-called unclaimed funds are the government's debt certificates from past years. Many certificate holders have not come to claim them for many years. The exact number is unknown because government officials fear that disclosing it might cause other incidents, so the total number is still unknown. However, it is estimated that the principal of the debt certificates is four million pounds sterling. The aforementioned huge sum is currently deposited in the Bank of England. The bank issued 68,000 notices, urging certificate holders to come and claim the overdue debts and interest. However, as a result, 12,700 letters were returned by the post office because they could not be delivered. Only about 1,200 letters could be re-sent to new addresses. It can be seen that about nine-tenths of the certificate holders are no longer aware of their whereabouts, having completely disregarded their personal property. Isn't that strange? There are 10,900 households with debt certificates, of which 40 households are entitled to more than 10,000 pounds sterling each. Among them, one household has as much as 187,593 pounds sterling, but no one has come to claim it. According to government officials' investigation, it is believed that these certificate holders are either old, deceased, sick, or living in foreign countries, having forgotten all that they had contributed to the country, or they forgot to include the purchase of government bonds in their wills before their death, so their descendants have no way of knowing. There is also a small group of people who are willing to sacrifice a little money to support the national treasury. These people are all very few nouveau riche. Two years ago, a British woman died in Marseille, France. She was poor and her funeral expenses were covered by relatives and friends. However, it was later discovered that she had bought 40,000 to 50,000 pounds of government bonds before her death, which had long expired and should be refunded. So they inquired with the Bank of England and found that there was indeed 56,000 pounds in her name that could be withdrawn. After deducting the expenses she had borrowed, her descendants suddenly made a fortune. According to the British Finance Ordinance of 1921, any government bonds that are not claimed after five years will be transferred to the national treasury. However, it is believed that the aforementioned debt is too large and confiscating it would harm the wealth of the people. Therefore, it is now being handled with flexibility, extending the deadline to ten years before it can be confiscated. It is also found that the aforementioned debt certificates are all of several types, such as Consols and Reduced Threes.

Travels in India (44) 142

— Ling Hua

On the 29th, the president of the Theological Society, Dr. and Secretary-General Dasha, requested a photo. Mrs. Cousins sent me a letter inviting me to the Asian Women's Association in Lahore and showed me the association's progress. Mrs. Cousins is an artist and writer who claims to be Irish, but has lived in India for a long time and is familiar with Eastern culture. Therefore, she has worked hard to help India and open the Asian Women's Association, having been imprisoned twice. When asked about history, I showed her various photos. When she saw those wearing Western clothes, she could not find who was me in the photos and blamed me, saying, "Why are you wearing foreign clothes? Who will recognize you as a Chinese person?" She disapproved of me not wearing Western clothes in India, but in the Nanyang area, almost no one wears Chinese clothes. Those who wear Chinese clothes are despised by everyone, because their spirits have been conquered for a long time. There are two Western female leaders in India, one is Miss Benson and the other is Mrs. Cousins, both Irish.

On this day, there was a lecture at the Asian Education Association, with about 3,000 listeners. There were two Chinese representatives, one of whom was elected chairman. There were also Japanese and Turkish representatives. Lawyer Mu Keji, a disciple of mine, also gave a lecture. His eyes were like lightning and his mouth was like a torrential river, his voice shaking the entire venue of 3,000 people. Mu is my Saint Paul.

On the 30th, I went to a women's school conference and met the celebrity Bao Guang, who said he was the highest person in the Indian academic world and wanted me to stay at his home. I could not go because I would be leaving Varanasi soon.

On the 31st, I took the train to Allahabad for three or four hours. The second-class fare was more than three yuan. I was guided by Lawyer Mu. We arrived at his in-laws' house at noon. Mu stood outside the door for a long time. His mother-in-law came out, but his wife could not come out to see me. I was surprised and asked him why. He replied, "This is our custom." I did not get to enter the house until the evening, which was also strange. In the evening, I took a walk in the city under the moon with university students. This city is very wide, clean, and has many trees. The air is clean, not only very different from the smoke and dust of Varanasi, but also more so than Calcutta. It is very similar to Penang. There are no British goods in the city, and few Chinese goods. It is said that there will be a strike tomorrow for a Gandhian-style mass movement. Lawyer Mu has three sons. I saw that the eyes of the youngest child were all blue, different from his father. Mu told me that our races have the same parents, but are different in black and white, perhaps from the father or from the mother. The eyes of the Indians prove that the Aryans are of the same race.

I find the strange customs in India very difficult, especially the matter of excretion. Since ancient times, people in the tropics have used their left hand to wipe themselves after defecating, so the left hand is considered unclean. However, what is strange is that they do not know how to use chopsticks to eat, but use their hands to grab food, but only with their right hand. We consider them unclean, but they say that those who use paper are unclean and impure. My friend occasionally uses paper himself, but dares not say it publicly, saying that his family and friends all say it is unclean and no one dares to approach him. People in Nanyang are obsessed with cleanliness because of the tropics, bordering on superstition. They use their hands to find feces and dig their feet, and at the same time use their hands to cook and eat. If these habits are not changed, it will be difficult to stand in today's scientific and cultural forest.

The Twists and Turns of the Hawthorne Detective Case (5) 143

— Cheng Xiaoqing

Having encountered this second accident, I was very clear in my mind that the person in front must have committed an illegal act, and the person behind must be a detective in pursuit. I was unfortunate to be caught in the middle, which caused the detective to misunderstand. I turned around and saw that the person chasing was already running close to me. The person was tall and wearing a black robe with no mandarin jacket. He was wearing a dark yellow striped tweed cap, which was pressed very low, but I could still see his dark and sinister face and a pair of round eyes under the electric light. He was clearly a plainclothes detective. My previous assumption had been confirmed. He must have misunderstood me. As he approached, I opened my mouth first and said, "Friend, you've made a mistake!" His right hand was holding a shiny nickel-plated pistol, the muzzle fixed on me. He coldly replied, "Who's made a mistake?" I said, "Don't you see that the person in front has turned the corner?" The burly man with the sinister face was very calm. He replied, "That's right, let him go." I said, "You can't let this person go." He said, "With you here, it's the same." I felt that his prejudice was very deep, and I couldn't find the right words to dispel his misunderstanding. I could only say, "You've really made a mistake. You can't let this person go. Chase after him quickly!" He said, "Won't you buy some candy to fool me?" I couldn't help but get annoyed and said, "You're stuck on the horns of a dilemma! This person is the criminal, and now he's getting away scot-free. You'll be responsible for that!" He also raised his voice and replied, "Catching the thief with the stolen goods is my responsibility. Isn't that thing on you?" As he said this, he took a step forward and pressed the muzzle of the gun against my chest. Suddenly, he reached out and touched the pocket of my left coat. In an instant, the necklace wrapped in a white cloth was in his hand. Then, a sinister smile appeared on his face. The triumphant state of frowning and squinting was hateful and ridiculous to see. Under these circumstances, if I followed my nature, I would risk everything and fight him. However, I had more experience and was confident that I had some scientific attitude. If I resisted him, I would not only be making the same mistake as him, but also risk losing the opportunity to clear myself. Because judging from this person's job, such measures were appropriate. Since he didn't know me, this misunderstanding was not easy to explain, and it was excusable in terms of the situation.

Commercial News

The Gold Market Shows a Slight Rising Trend 144

Initial Weakness and Subsequent Strength

Yesterday, the 5th, was the second day of the Spring Races, and the gold exchange was still only open for half a day in the morning. The benchmark gold price rebounded and showed a rising trend, but it was weak in the morning and then gradually strengthened, eventually becoming slightly softer. It is estimated that there were fluctuations in the market due to the divergent trends in overseas silver markets, with prices falling in England and rising in the United States. Therefore, the gold price also fell. Afterwards, the Bao Fang was diligent, and although the foreign exchange quotation increased by half a notch, the internal market was still stable. It is said that the external market was loose and the internal market was tight, and the rumors in the market began to subside, so the market turned gentle. The price has exceeded 40 taels. Afterwards, the supply exceeded demand, and the market was slightly softer, but there were not many transactions in the market.

There were slight fluctuations. The opening price for June was slightly lower by 7 cents, at 737 taels, because the large bar price fell by one-sixteenth, while the silver price rose by one-eighth. There were no increases or decreases in private telegrams. Jiaxing North and South Silkworms Entering Third Molt 157

Cold weather prevents molting, development is very slow.

During the seeding period, due to the cold weather, the hatching of silkworms was delayed, with only 60% of the seeds hatching. As the silkworms were about to enter their third molt, the weather remained cold and rainy, causing the silkworms to be unable to molt and the development of late silkworms to be delayed.

Automobile News

Special Article

Advantages of 1931 Model New Cars 165

— Dai

Various new cars of the 1931 model have been launched one after another. Observing the improvements made by various manufacturers in the production of new cars, the special points which are particularly noteworthy are listed below to inform the readers of this publication.

Low Price: Various new cars of the 1931 model have been displayed on the market. Looking at their advantages, the most amazing thing is the low price. Currently, a good car can be purchased for USD 1,000 or less. Is this something we could have anticipated beforehand? Based on the history of cars, the initial price of new cars in the past was the highest. The price of the same car today is less than 1,000 yuan, and eight-cylinder cars are even flooding the market. The power of these cars is unprecedented, and the appearance of the new cars, both inside and outside, is amazing. The obvious stripes, the smooth exterior, and the clean driver's seat are all admirable. They are truly affordable and high-quality cars.

Beautiful Colors: The colors added to the car body have also greatly improved compared to the past, and the colors of each part are coordinated and consistent. The so-called coordination is not only the appearance, but also the interior. Even the scattered accessories have good-looking colors, reflecting each other without being annoying. Such results would not be possible without the careful research of the factory workers. The construction method is simplified where possible, and reduced where possible, which allows car owners to purchase cars at low prices. In short, the improvements of the new cars of the 1931 model are indeed many, and all of them are surprising. It can be seen that the progress of cars is rapid.

More Cars: In terms of the cars produced by various factories in the past year, there is obviously a new trend, that is, more cylinders. Recalling that in 1929, six-cylinder cars accounted for 60% of the total number of cars produced, while in 1930, eight-cylinder cars accounted for 60%. Compared with each other, they are inversely proportional. It can be seen that the recent trend in car manufacturing is towards more cylinders. With more cylinders, the power of the car itself will naturally increase. The improvement of the pistons and the expansion of the combustion chamber all increase the power of the car.

Transmission System: Analyzing the new cars of the 1931 model, there are 20 types of chassis with four-speed transmissions and 63 types with three-speed transmissions. There is one type where all gears use live gears, and ten types where live gears are only used in the highest or second speed. The improvement of the transmission system in the 1931 model is particularly noteworthy and worth discussing, and has a great impact on business. In addition, the efforts to increase the number of cylinders have even led to the introduction of 16-cylinder cars, and the results are very excellent. This is a major milestone in the history of cars. The improvement of the handle is also sufficient to increase the power of the car.

Other Various Things: The improvements of the new cars of various factories are as described above. In addition, there are many more, and the most satisfactory thing is the sun-shading windshield. Although low-priced cars also have this kind of windshield installed, windshields made of thin glass have become common. Soon, society will need this kind of car. The improvement of the speedometer allows the driver to know the speed while driving, rather than having to observe the speedometer in detail as in the past, and it is quite accurate. There are many other advantages, but due to space limitations, I cannot describe them all here. I can only be brief.

Dodge's Reputation for Sixteen Years 166

— Ying

Dodge is also one of the famous American car factories. Recently, its business has also developed quite well. Since its establishment, it has been sixteen years. During these sixteen years, the factory authorities have worked hard and finally won considerable reputation for the excellent quality of their products and the effectiveness of their operations. Recently, they held a sixteen-week anniversary celebration, which was quite lively. The development of Dodge in the past sixteen years is briefly described below for commemoration, which is also welcomed by readers.

The First Car: On November 14, 1930, the American Dodge car factory held a sixteen-week anniversary celebration, because the Dodge car factory has been established for sixteen years. Recalling sixteen years ago, in 1915, Dodge cars began to be displayed at the car exhibition meeting to meet the society. The development of Dodge in the past sixteen years is quite mysterious. Although there is no sufficient proof that Dodge has a considerable foundation and credibility today, one thing can be told to the readers, that is, the first car produced by Dodge is still running on the streets today, even though it has been sixteen years. We can see it in Nashville, Tennessee. If we make a total of the distance traveled by this car, it has traveled 350,000 miles in sixteen years. The Dodge factory's agent who used to sell this car is still the Dodge factory's distributor today, and the number of cars sold by this person in sixteen years is countless.

The Origin of Reputation: The only reason why Dodge's reputation has a solid foundation is that the factory strives to make the products have considerable value and also strives to save money for car buyers. The main point to achieve this goal is good planning, excellent raw materials, and highly skilled car makers. Otherwise, it is not enough to have affordable and high-quality cars. Looking at the distance traveled by the first Dodge car, it can cross the Earth six times, and the car itself has not had major damage. It can be seen that its excellent performance has been achieved during the driving. This kind of service spirit has been the same for sixteen years and has not changed much so far. When making cars, raw materials must be selected from the best, and the price must be very low after the cars are made. As for Dodge cars still getting social credit today, it is because the new cars have been improved year by year, and the appearance and content can satisfy customers. During these sixteen years, the Dodge car engine has been reformed year by year and has made a lot of progress. It is indeed a good car. Recalling the initial release of the first car that year, it is unimaginable to have such amazing results today. Compared with the past, not only is the material better, but also the horsepower is more, the driving is faster, and the safety problem has also been greatly improved.

Total Number of Cars Sold: During these sixteen years, the number of cars sold by the Dodge factory has reached 2.5 million, and the price paid by car owners has reached more than USD 400 billion. Among the factories in the United States, the number of cars sold is so large and the credit is so stable, which can be called unique. As for making car owners feel satisfied, it is even more a matter of ability. Comparing today's cars with the first car produced at the beginning of the company, the improvements are even more overwhelming. The new cars of each year have many improvements, so Dodge cars can be called perfect today. Regardless of other things, the beauty of the car, the appropriateness of the length, the richness of the power, and the convenience of driving are all admirable. The goal of the factory in making cars is still to strive for affordable, high-quality, and more refined products. Therefore, the new cars of the future will be better than today. There is no doubt.

History of the Development of the British Automobile Industry 167

— Song Yu

Comparison of Thirty Years Ago and Now

Mr. Fogel Bincley said that thirty years ago, all the private cars, commercial freight cars, and rented buses in Great Britain totaled less than 3,000. At that time, the total number of workers manufacturing cars in the country was only about 2,000. Now the situation is very different. Just in terms of workers manufacturing cars, the total number of workers required in each car factory is at least 500,000. Therefore, many people say that in the current era of commercial decline and the increasing number of unemployed, it is very hopeful to use the automobile industry to alleviate this shortcoming.

No one knows what the speed and durability of cars were at the beginning of the 20th century. The Golden Arrow car was a magical thing. Twelve-cylinder and sixteen-cylinder cars had not yet been designed. At that time, the automobile industry was in its infancy. France had only 2,897 cars at this time, of which 543 were made for industrial experiments. The French automobile industry progressed very quickly only after 1896. A lot of experimental fees were spent. In 1895, the French drove from Paris to Bordeaux and then back to Paris, creating a 744-mile car race record. The car that won the championship had a top piston, a large carburetor, and a very ugly appearance. On rough and uneven roads, it averaged 15 miles per hour.

The Germans paid great attention to the automobile manufacturing industry. In the new century, German engineers spent a lot of effort trying to use cars as a medium of transportation to seek a revolution in transportation. The effect was very good in seven years. Just in 1907, 27,026 cars were built. In 1900, there were only 600 cars in the United States, worth USD 1,290,000. At that time, Henry Ford was just a young mechanic dreaming of building his own car. Sure enough, he became the world's largest car manufacturer. Datcheliwu was a wealthy river city waiting for the climax of the automobile industry to arrive. Circuit judges rode horses back and forth, and there was a fire engine holding the highest speed record.

Thirty years ago, Great Britain began to manufacture cars. British car manufacturers spent a lot of money like the French. In this early and unstable start, everyone wanted to hold the qualification of the leader of the automobile manufacturing industry. In this way, everyone inevitably competed, followed by competition for raw materials such as metal materials, oil, rubber, and steel. This is the first scene after the invention of the car and has not stopped until now.

Page 20

Since 1900, countries have used their capital and capabilities to seek sales in foreign markets. Laws to protect domestic markets have also been passed at the same time. Thousands of dollars have been spent to obtain speed and endurance records. Car travel and steamships and trains have competed with each other and opened up many new places. This is mostly what has happened in the last thirty years. In the early years, when British industry was still wavering, there were often laws restricting the development of the automobile industry. For example, between 1896 and 1904, cars weighing more than three tons were not allowed to run on the roads, and freight cars were even prohibited. In 1900, the Great Britain and Ireland Automobile Club, which is now the Royal Automobile Club, launched a 1,000-mile British car trip in order to arouse the pleasure of car travel. The cars in this car trip team patronized various cities, including Scotland. When the car arrived in a town, it was warmly welcomed. The miners in the cellar abandoned their shovels and came to the ground to see this novel machine that burned gasoline. The driver seemed effortless, so the celebrations of the people were everywhere. Banks and shops were mostly closed. No matter where it was or who it was, everyone was very interested in this new invention of the 20th century machine.

This parade proved to the public that cars were practical items for transportation. By 1905, the number of cars in Great Britain had increased sevenfold. In 1907, car factories produced 1,000 cars and commercial freight cars per month. In 1910, the annual car output was 14,000. Ten years later, there were 80 car manufacturers in England, Scotland, and Ireland. However, only one car factory was in Ireland, in Belfast. The factories employed a total of 40,000 workers. This 80 car manufacturers were established in a certain year 20 years ago. 30 of them still use the old names. The rest have either ceased operations or merged with other car factories, or changed to new brands.

Report

Ford and General Motors Business Reports 168

— Guo Xiang

The former's net profit was more than $55 million, while the latter increased cash by more than $51 million.

1930 was the most economically panicked era in the United States in over a decade. All industries were withering, the market was depressed, the number of vagrants increased sharply, and purchasing power decreased sharply. Coupled with the impact of unemployment throughout the world, there was no way out for exports. For a year, the society was panicked, and everyone expected that the domestic manufacturing leader would have huge losses. Unexpectedly, things turned out differently. Not only did the manufacturing giant not show weakness, but the huge profits it made were truly astonishing. This point allows us to see that American industry has entered adulthood. Here, I will write down the business conditions of the above-mentioned two major automobile manufacturing companies last year.

Ford: In the past twelve months, the company has won a total net profit of 55 million US dollars, shipped a total of 1.5 million vehicles, and stored 300 million dollars in circulating cash, which is less than the previous year. Its profit was more than 81 million dollars, and a total of more than 1.95 million cars were produced. The company's current economy is extremely strong, and its business is particularly stable. Compared with the difficult situation of lacking cash ten years ago, it is now a world apart. This year's business has shown a turning point. The goods shipped by the company in February have increased by 35% to 41% compared with the same period last year. In March, a total of 95,000 vehicles were produced. This month, an average of 7,000 passenger and freight vehicles can be produced per day. It is expected that the 20 millionth Ford vehicle will be produced on the 14th of this month. The company's two major factories in Dirt Earth City employ a total of 83,425 people, an increase of more than 10,000 people compared with the same period last year. Ford is still making every effort to carry out development plans, such as the new factory in India, the rubber factory in South America, and the recent purchase of a large number of cargo steamships.

General Motors Joint Company: Although trade last year decreased by 34.6% compared with the previous year, cash reserves increased by more than 51 million yuan. The total profit for the year was 151 million yuan, and each share could be divided into 3 yuan and 25 cents, which was less than the previous year's dividend of 5 yuan and 49 cents per share. However, it is fortunate that there is still such a profit in this era of oppression. The company's general manager, Mr. Shi Long, said that the company's economic situation is becoming more and more consolidated. The estimated total assets are more than 130 million and 15,800,000 gold. The annual income exceeds the expenditure, and each group unit cooperates and manages effectively. He is quite optimistic about the future.

Overview of Hunan-Hubei Road Administration 170

— Wu Fei

The road construction in Hunan and Hubei provinces is particularly important due to the mountainous terrain. Therefore, the authorities of the two provinces are paying close attention to either planning future projects or striving to realize traffic, all in the hope of facilitating people's transportation and developing industry and commerce. The following is a record of the road administration surveys of the two provinces.

Hunan Province: The Hunan Provincial authorities, due to financial relations, are prioritizing and constructing road administration projects in order of urgency. According to its future projects, there are eleven lines: (1) On the Hunan-Hubei West Line, first complete the Weijiang Bridge in the Ningyi section and the Niulutan Bridge in the Yichang section, as well as the bridge paving sand from Shande Mountain to Changde Duhe Xiamen, and the unfinished projects such as the station houses and road sheds in the two sections still require funding of 245,522 yuan, which will take about five months to complete. Secondly, construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Changde via Lizhou to Jinnan. This section is 205 li in length and requires 658,660 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. (2) On the Hunan-Hubei East Suixian, first complete the various projects from Huanghuashi to Gaoqiao, which are 70 li in length and require 150,000 yuan, which will take about two months to complete. Secondly, construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Gaoqiao to Pingjiang, which is 120 li in length and requires 335,472 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. (3) The Hunan-Jiangxi Line must complete the various projects from Changsha to Yonganshi, which are 60 li in length and require 52,438 yuan, which will take about two months to complete. (4) The Hunan-Guangdong Line will complete the various projects from Chenxian via Yizhang to the Guangdong border, which are 105 li in length and require 224,263 yuan, which will take about four months to complete. (5) The Hunan-Guangxi Line will first complete the various projects from Hengyang to Hongqiao. This section still requires 84,084 yuan, which will take about two months to complete. Secondly, construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Hongqiao Jing Yongzhou Lishanpu to the Guangxi border. This section is 300 li in length and requires 834,496 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. (6) The Hunan-Guizhou Line will first complete the various projects from Taohuaping to Gaoshashi. This section is 120 li in length and will require 525,024 yuan, which will take about six months to complete. Secondly, construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Gaoshashi to Jiangkoushi. This section is 140 li in length and requires 908,920 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. (7) The Hunan-Sichuan Line will first construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Xiangxiang to Qiaotoushi. This section is 160 li in length and requires 519,480 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. Secondly, construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Qiaotoushi Prefecture to Xinhua. This section is 150 li in length and requires 414,576 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. (8) The Liu Ruzhi Branch Line will complete the various projects from Youxian to Chaling, which are 90 li in length and still require 133,112 yuan, which will take about three months to complete. (9) The Changhong Branch Line will first complete the various projects from Taoyuan to Xintianyiyi. This section is 120 li in length and still requires 411,684 yuan, which will take about six months to complete. Secondly, construct the roadbed and bridge culvert project from Xinli to Jieting, which is 100 li in length and requires 287,352 yuan, which will take about twelve months to complete. (10) The Changlin Branch Line will construct the various projects from Yueyang to Chenglingji, which are 15 li in length and require 66,470 yuan, which will take about four months to complete. (11) The exploration team will organize two exploration teams to explore the routes from Taoyuan to Yuanling and from Taohuaping to Hongjiang. This year will require 24,912 yuan. The above projects will require a total of 5,879,375 yuan.

Hubei Province: The northern Hubei provincial roads, such as the eastern Hubei, western Hubei, southern Hubei, and northern Hubei roads, have already started construction, but only a few of them can be opened to traffic. The following is a record of the roads that can be opened to traffic in the four lines: (1) Those belonging to eastern Hubei are the roads that start from Hankou and pass through Hankou Hengdian Huangban Puanzhai Liuzigou Xinzhou Linshanhe Fanggaoping Shanbahe Chishui Guangji Qingjiangpu, which are 671 li in length. Currently, traffic only reaches Liuzigang. Another branch road passes through Liuzigang, Songbu, Qiting, Zhongguanyi, to Macheng County, and more than 80 li have been opened to traffic. (2) Those belonging to northern Hubei, such as the Xianghua Road, start from Xiaogan Huayuan and pass through Anlu, Pinglin, Maping, Xihe, Suixian, Lishan, Tangxian, Xinglongji, Zaoyang, Shuanggou, Fancheng, Taipingdian, Laohekou, and 670 li have been opened to traffic. The Xianghe Road starts from Xiangyang and passes through Ouzhen, Yicheng, Kongshi, Lexiang, Nanqiao, Jingmen, Tuanling, Jianyang, Shilipu, Sifangpu, near Huikou Bridge, Jiangling, and Heshi to the north, which is 490 li in length. The Yiwu Branch Road passes through Yicheng via Zhudian to Wuanzhen, which is 60 li in length. (3) Those belonging to western Hubei are the Hanyi Road, which currently starts from Anlu Station on the Xianghua Road and passes through Yitangzhen and Geputan Changjiangbu, and 100 li have been opened to traffic. The roads to Yichang stations have not yet started construction. (4) Those belonging to Zhengnan, such as the Wujin Road, run from Wuchang city through Baishazhou and Shazui to Jinkouzhen, which is 60 li in length. The Wubao Road starts from Wuchang city and passes through Hongshan, Lujiagang, Youfangling to Baozixie, which is 90 li in length. The Wuhu Road starts from Wuchang city and passes through Xiaxinhe Xujiapeng, Qingshan, Baji, to Baihuzhen, which is 60 li in length.

Translated News

World Car Scraps 171

— Pei

Buick's new cars sold well for a time: From July 1930 to the end of last year, in these five months, the number of straight-eight cylinder new cars sold by General Motors was very large, more than one and a half times the number sold by other competitors in a year. In 1930, the number of Buick's new cars sold was 49,464, while the number sold by its competitors in a year was 31,275. This factory is the runner-up in the manufacture of straight-eight cylinder cars. According to Mr. Churchill, the sales director of Buick Motor Company, although the sales figures for the new cars in January this year have not yet been released, judging from the delivery of goods from the factory, the sales figures should still be ranked first and will not fall. Mr. Qiu also said that Buick Company recently announced that the current 1931 straight-eight cylinder cars will continue to be in circulation in the summer and autumn of this year. Those who have new cars on August 1 will be held slowly, so the sales of this new car this spring can be compared with last year.

The Pope's car has a throne: The Rome Milan Automobile Club recently donated a car worth 50,000 yuan to Pope Bishi. This car is magnificent and unprecedented. There is a throne in the car, all plated with gold. When the emperor drives through the city, he always sits in it and looks around for pleasure. This throne can also be removed when necessary and replaced with two seats with high cushions and thick compartments, which are extremely luxurious, so that the Pope can drive and sit with guests. The backs of the cars are decorated with gold, silver, and ivory, and the curtains are made in the Venetian style.

Italian Thousand Mile Car Race: The world's most unique and longest car race is held in Italy every year, with a length of 1,000 miles. This car race originated from the Briss Automobile Club. Each race starts from here and passes through Jiluona Fuluo Laien Rome Anguona to Baoluona Tuolei Fusha Faner Tuowensheng Shifuluona and other places, and finally returns to the starting point of Brissxi. The most unique thing about this competition is that the roads that the competition cars pass through can still be used by other non-competition vehicles during the competition. Later, newspapers published comments requesting residents to automatically abandon this road so that the competition could proceed smoothly. This request was approved by the public, so this year there are more vehicles participating in the competition than in previous years. As many as 140 vehicles of various types participated.

The Remarkable Plymouth Car: The Indian Gorge Road of the Carolina Smoky Mountains has always been known as a dangerous road for travel. Four cars have never set foot on it. This began with the remarkable Plymouth car. Mr. Hao Fu, the owner of a mountain resort in the Smoky Mountains, drove this car from Gatuolinbai in four hours and five minutes. Although the entire journey is only 24 miles long, other vehicles have never reached the other 10 miles except by walking and riding. The mountain is about 5,500 feet high.

Building Automobile Roads in Africa: The remote and smoke-filled hinterland of Africa, where people rarely set foot, now has a network of automobile roads connected to the outside world. The various local products are generally transported to various places using modern transportation methods. The locals who used to carry goods on their backs and travel long distances are now replaced by automobiles. The camel's journey is also replaced by automobiles, which are comfortable and fast. The famous Nile and Congo rivers in Africa are now connected by roads, and there is a regular automobile postal service.

Estimate of US Automobile Tax: The average amount of US automobile tax in 1930 was US$33. This estimate was published by the California Automobile Association and is roughly the same. This average automobile tax of 33 US dollars has increased by 14% compared with the previous year, because the automobile tax levied at that time was only 28 US dollars and 56 cents.

Please go to the accounting department of this museum to collect them from the 12th of this month. The Automobile News Department
